            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadOneTrustScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();

            if (!shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            preloadBannerSdk();

            ONE_TRUST_LIBRARIES.forEach((library) => {
                loadScript(library.url, "text/javascript", library.options);
            });

            if (country === "US") {
                loadCCPAAddon();
            }
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithOneTrustEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithOneTrustEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithOneTrustEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            script.setAttribute("data-domain-script", DATA_DOMAIN_SCRIPT);

            return script;
        }

        function loadCCPAAddon() {
            loadScript(CCPA_ADDON.url, "text/javascript", CCPA_ADDON.options);
        }

        function preloadBannerSdk() {
            const link = document.createElement("link");
            link.href = BANNER_SDK.url;
            link.rel = "preload";
            link.as = "script";

            document.head.appendChild(link);
        }

        function oneTrustLoaded() {
            return !!(window.OneTrust || window.OneTrustStub);
        }

        console.debug('OneTrust setup', countriesWithOneTrustEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !oneTrustLoaded()) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!oneTrustLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (function () {
        function shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            const countriesWithKetchEnabled = {"countries":["IN","HU","SG"]};
            if (!countriesWithKetchEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithKetchEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }
            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithKetchEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }


        function loadKetchScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            if (!shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            window.semaphore = window.semaphore || [];

            window.ketch = function () {
                window.semaphore.push(arguments);
            };

            var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(document.location.search);
            var property = urlParams.has("property") ? urlParams.get("property") : "website_smart_tag";

            var scriptElement = document.createElement("script");
            scriptElement.type = "text/javascript";
            scriptElement.src = "https://global.ketchcdn.com/web/v2/config/fandom/" + property + "/boot.js";
            scriptElement.defer = scriptElement.async = true;

            document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(scriptElement);
        }

        function ketchLoaded() {
            return !!window.ketch;
        }

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !ketchLoaded()) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!ketchLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (async function () {
        // const AIRGAP_URL = '<script
        // data-cfasync="false"
        // src=""
        const AIRGAP_URL = 'https://transcend-cdn.com/cm/54b0c313-5d22-47e5-92fd-f979a37d1ad0/airgap.js';
        const countriesWithAirgapEnabled = [];

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {

            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadAirgapScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            const enabled = shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) || airgapScriptForced();

            if (!enabled) {
                return;
            }

            loadScript(AIRGAP_URL, "text/javascript", {
                'data-cfasync': false
            });
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithAirgapEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function airgapScriptForced() {
            return window.location.search.includes('icPreferredCMP=airgap');
        }

        function shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithAirgapEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithAirgapEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            return script;
        }

        console.debug('Airgap setup', countriesWithAirgapEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        let geo = getGeo();

        if (geo === null) {
            geo = await waitForGeo();
        }

        if (geo) {
            loadAirgapScripts(geo);
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
	const useMaxDefaultContentWidth = Boolean(false);

	const defaultContentWidth = useMaxDefaultContentWidth ? 'expanded' : 'collapsed';

	let contentWidthPreference;

	try {
		contentWidthPreference = localStorage.getItem('contentwidth') || defaultContentWidth;
	} catch (e) {
		contentWidthPreference = defaultContentWidth;
	}

	if ( contentWidthPreference === 'expanded' ) {
		document.documentElement.classList.add('is-content-expanded');
	}
</script>

													<script data-name="featured-video-mapped-to-wiki">
	(function () {
		// we can't use mw.config here because it's too early so we need to pass this data in different way
		const videoDetails = {
			mapping: {"mediaId":"sXWp3rZ0","connatixPlaylistId":"36081eca-e784-4e30-87c3-133cf673e447","impressionsPerSession":4},
			impressionsPerSession: 4,
		};
		const videoBridgeCountries = ["AE","AG","AL","AM","AR","AT","AU","AZ","BA","BB","BD","BG","BH","BN","BO","BR","BS","BY","CA","CH","CL","CN","CO","CR","CU","CY","CZ","DE","DK","DO","DZ","EC","EE","EG","ES","FI","FR","GB","GE","GF","GG","GH","GP","GR","GT","GU","GY","HK","HN","HR","HU","ID","IE","IL","IM","IN","IQ","IR","IS","IT","JE","JM","JO","JP","KE","KG","KH","KR","KW","KY","KZ","LA","LB","LK","LT","LU","LV","LY","MA","MD","ME","MK","MM","MN","MO","MQ","MT","MU","MV","MX","MY","NG","NI","NO","NP","NZ","OM","PA","PE","PH","PK","PL","PR","PS","PT","PY","QA","RE","RO","RS","RU","SA","SC","SE","SG","SI","SK","SV","TD","TH","TN","TR","TT","TW","UA","US","UY","UZ","VE","VI","VN","ZA","ZW"];
		const tier3VideoBridgeCountries = ["GB","BE","NL","DE","AU","MX","AR","FR","MD","CA","ES","IT","PE","CO","CL","NZ"];
		let hasVideoOnPage = null;

		function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
			const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
			return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
		}

		function hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki() {
			const impressionsSoFar = Number(getCookieValue('playerImpressionsInWiki')) || 0;
			const allowedImpressions = Number(videoDetails.impressionsPerSession);

			return impressionsSoFar >= allowedImpressions;
		}

		function getCountryCode() {
			try {
				return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo'))).country.toLowerCase();
			} catch {
				return null;
			}
		}

		function isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() {
			const countryCode = getCountryCode();

			if (!countryCode) {
				return false;
			}

			// If it's a default mapping, then check the country whitelist from the default mapping.
			if (videoDetails?.mapping?.isDefaultMapping) {
				// If the wiki is classified as a tier3 wiki, then check the country whitelist from the tier3VideoBridge whitelist.
				const allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis = tier3VideoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedTier3CountryCode) {
					return allowedTier3CountryCode.toLowerCase();
				})

				return allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			} else {
				// If not a default mapping wiki (so it's a wiki mapping), then check the country whitelist from the videoBridge whitelist
				const allowedCountries = videoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedCountryCode) {
					return allowedCountryCode.toLowerCase();
				});

				return allowedCountries.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			}
		}

		window.fandomIsVideoPossible = function () {
			if (hasVideoOnPage === null) {
				hasVideoOnPage =
					videoDetails.mapping &&
					isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() &&
					!hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki();
			}

			return hasVideoOnPage;
		};

		window.canPlayVideo = function () {
			return window.fandomIsVideoPossible()
		};

		if (!window.canPlayVideo()) {
			document.body.classList.add('no-featured-video');
		} else {
			document.body.classList.add('has-featured-video');
		}
	})();
</script>

<section class="pi-item pi-group pi-border-color pi-collapse pi-collapse-open">
	<h2 class="pi-item pi-header pi-secondary-font pi-item-spacing pi-secondary-background"><span class="df-header">Devil Fruit</span></h2>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfname">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Japanese Name:</h3>

<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Magnet-Magnet Fruit</div></div></td></tr>
<tr><td><div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfmeaning"><span class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Meaning:</span>
<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Magnetism</div></div></td></tr>
<tr><td><div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dftype"><span class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Type:</span>
<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Paramecia" title="Paramecia">Paramecia</a></div></div></td></tr>

<p><b>Eustass "Captain" Kid</b><sup id="cite_ref-c594p11_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c594p11-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> is a notorious <a href="/wiki/Pirate" title="Pirate">pirate</a> from the <a href="/wiki/South_Blue" title="South Blue">South Blue</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Pirate_Captain" title="Pirate Captain">captain</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Kid_Pirates" title="Kid Pirates">Kid Pirates</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> He is one of twelve pirates who are referred to as the "<a href="/wiki/Worst_Generation" title="Worst Generation">Worst Generation</a>".<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Kid first appeared at the <a href="/wiki/Sabaody_Archipelago" title="Sabaody Archipelago">Sabaody Archipelago</a> at the same time <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> and <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">his crew</a> arrived. Both were described as members of the "Eleven Supernovas", pirates who had congregated on the island who all had a bounty of more than <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>100,000,000. After briefly fighting alongside Luffy while escaping an attack by the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a>, he fled the archipelago and would later spectate the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Summit War of Marineford</a> alongside the other Supernovas.
</p><p>During Luffy's two years of training, Kid challenged one of the <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Four Emperors</a>, <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a>, but lost one of his arms in the process.<sup id="cite_ref-c928_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c928-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> He attempted to form an alliance with the <a href="/wiki/On_Air_Pirates" title="On Air Pirates">On Air Pirates</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hawkins_Pirates" title="Hawkins Pirates">Hawkins Pirates</a> to challenge the <a href="/wiki/Red_Hair_Pirates" title="Red Hair Pirates">Red Hair Pirates</a> once more, but the alliance fell apart after an attack from another Emperor, <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-c677_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c677-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c795_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c795-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c954_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c954-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> which led to his imprisonment at <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano Country</a> where he would eventually reunite with Luffy. Though nominally acting in self-interest towards vengeance and glory, Kid's assistance towards the <a href="/wiki/Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai_Alliance" title="Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance">Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance</a> was instrumental in defeating Kaidou, Big Mom and the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a>.
</p><p>After leaving Wano, Kid and his crew arrived at <a href="/wiki/Elbaph" title="Elbaph">Elbaph</a> and decided to challenge Shanks once more. However, the entire crew and their <a href="/wiki/Victoria_Punk" title="Victoria Punk">ship</a> were decimated by Shanks and his allies, <a href="/wiki/Dorry" title="Dorry">Dorry</a> and <a href="/wiki/Brogy" title="Brogy">Brogy</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c1079_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1079-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>Kid was originally introduced with a bounty of <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>315,000,000, largely due to a high number of civilian casualties caused by him and his crew, thus exceeding <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a>'s when they first arrived at the Sabaody Archipelago.<sup id="cite_ref-c498p19_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c498p19-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> Sometime during the timeskip, his bounty was raised from 315,000,000 to <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>470,000,000.<sup id="cite_ref-c677p3_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c677p3-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> Kid's bounty was eventually raised to <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>3,000,000,000 for his role in defeating <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a> of the Four Emperors alongside <a href="/wiki/Trafalgar_D._Water_Law" title="Trafalgar D. Water Law">Trafalgar Law</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Raid_on_Onigashima" title="Raid on Onigashima">Raid on Onigashima</a>. 
</p><p>Due to his actions, Kid can be considered a minor ally during the <a href="/wiki/Sabaody_Archipelago_Arc" title="Sabaody Archipelago Arc">Sabaody Archipelago Arc</a> as well as a major ally during the <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country_Arc" title="Wano Country Arc">Wano Country Arc</a>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Appearance">Appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D1&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Kid is a tall, muscular man with light skin and short spiky bright red hair, resembling flames. His nose has a particular shape, being quite pointed and having little protrusions on both sides. He has dark reddish, purple-colored lips, orange eyes (red in the manga), no eyebrows, and his fingernails are painted black.
</p><p>He dresses in an extravagant attire consisting of black and yellow lizard-print pants with a red fringe, motorcycle boots, and a blue sash under a green belt fastened by a large circular buckle with a four-leaf clover-like pattern in the middle. He also has a slim bandolier, also with minuscule bolts that go diagonally over his right shoulder then ties to his waist, where he keeps a dagger with a Japanese-style hilt and what appears to be a flintlock gun. He also has gold bangles around both wrists.
</p><p>He wears a pair of studded, square shaped yellow goggles with purple lenses on his forehead, and a large fur captain's coat over his bare muscular torso. The dark brown coat is adorned with spikes on its shoulders lined in maroon. The collar of the coat is extremely flared and wide. He typically wears this coat with his right arm in its sleeve and his left arm under the coat itself.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/SBS_Volume_64" title="SBS Volume 64">SBS Volume 64</a>, Oda drew the Supernovas as children. Kid is shown with spikier and more spread-out hair, similar to a lion's mane. He also wore larger and rounder goggles and did not have dark lips. He was depicted tinkering with a toy robot with a wrench. His blue sleeveless shirt has a sewn patch, like his yellow striped pants, and has a patch.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After the timeskip, he is shown with slightly longer hair that appears to be pushed back. He also has a large scar that drags from the left side of his forehead, goes down his neck and another smaller one that goes through his left eye. There are two parallel scars on his lower right arm and stomach. He lost his left arm to just above the elbow during the two-year timeskip in a battle against the <a href="/wiki/Red_Hair_Pirates" title="Red Hair Pirates">Red Hair Pirates</a> first mate <a href="/wiki/Benn_Beckman" title="Benn Beckman">Benn Beckman</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-c928_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c928-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-sbs107_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs107-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> and until his imprisonment by the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a>, he replaced it with a mechanical one that is somehow connected to his nervous system, shown by the presence of several metallic wires embedded directly into his skin. The mechanical arm was damaged in his fight against <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a>, and later stripped from him to disarm him and put him at further disadvantage if he rebelled against his captor. His attire consists of his trademark spotted pants, a black opened vest, held down by a belted war kilt. He also has a long dark red coat, worn over his shoulders. He appears to have become more muscular and also has scars on his right forearm, left pectoral, and on the left side of his abdomen. He no longer wears any impractical jewelry.<sup id="cite_ref-c677p3_6-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c677p3-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During the <a href="/wiki/Raid_on_Onigashima" title="Raid on Onigashima">raid on Onigashima</a>, he assembled a new mechanical arm.<sup id="cite_ref-c974_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c974-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> It was later temporarily severed due to <a href="/wiki/Basil_Hawkins" title="Basil Hawkins">Hawkins'</a> <a href="/wiki/Wara_Wara_no_Mi" title="Wara Wara no Mi">damage transfer</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> but was ultimately repaired.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Gallery">Gallery</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D2&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Video_Games">Video Games</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D4&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>

</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 127px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 127px; height: 127px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e6/Eustass_Kid%27s_Episode_917_Wanted_Poster.png/revision/latest?cb=20201105103149" class="image"><img alt="Eustass Kid&#39;s Episode 917 Wanted Poster" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="104" height="105" data-image-name="Eustass Kid&#39;s Episode 917 Wanted Poster.png" data-image-key="Eustass_Kid%27s_Episode_917_Wanted_Poster.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e6/Eustass_Kid%27s_Episode_917_Wanted_Poster.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/104?cb=20201105103149" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Kid's non-canon bounty poster from <a href="/wiki/Episode_917" title="Episode 917">Episode 917</a> (also used in series' merchandising).
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 127px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 127px; height: 127px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a4/HEADLINERS.png/revision/latest?cb=20171009155634" class="image"><img alt="HEADLINERS" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="105" height="105" data-image-name="HEADLINERS.png" data-image-key="HEADLINERS.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a4/HEADLINERS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/105?cb=20171009155634" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Kid and Trafalgar D. Water Law before timeskip on the cover of the disc <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Island_Song_Collection" title="One Piece Island Song Collection">One Piece Island Song Collection</a></i>.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 127px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 127px; height: 127px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/81/Seventh_Eyecatcher_Kid_Hanafuda.png/revision/latest?cb=20230402025553" class="image"><img alt="Seventh Eyecatcher Kid Hanafuda" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="105" height="59" data-image-name="Seventh Eyecatcher Kid Hanafuda.png" data-image-key="Seventh_Eyecatcher_Kid_Hanafuda.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/81/Seventh_Eyecatcher_Kid_Hanafuda.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/105?cb=20230402025553" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Kid's hanafuda card in the 7th set of <a href="/wiki/Eyecatchers" title="Eyecatchers">Eyecatchers</a>.
</div></span></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality">Personality</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D6&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Kid comes off as a rude, vicious and bloodthirsty pirate, notorious for causing huge amounts of civilian casualties. Whenever feeling like he is being mocked or insulted, even though a glance, he is quick to resort to violence.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> In fact, Kid can be so violent that he considers the choice of not immediately killing someone in his direct vicinity an act of gratitude.<sup id="cite_ref-c950_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c950-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> He also seems to be cruel even when not provoked, crucifying another defeated pirate crew just because he deemed them too weak to roam around in the New World.<sup id="cite_ref-c594_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c594-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> Kid is overall highly temperamental and has little patience with anyone getting in his way, although he is capable of restraining his anger in certain situations.<sup id="cite_ref-c500_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c500-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> Kid can also be very petty, having killed countless civilians for merely mocking or laughing at him for his dream of being the Pirate King, killing several pirates in the New World for being weak, and attempting to kill Shanks' fleet solely to goad the Emperor to fight him.  
</p><p>Kid is bold, cocky and fearless, known to run into danger regardless of the consequences.<sup id="cite_ref-c979_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c979-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> This is particularly the case when dealing with people who previously wronged him, at which point Kid will throw all caution to the wind and go straight for revenge.<sup id="cite_ref-c980_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c980-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> He does not hesitate to challenge even the <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Four Emperors</a>, having previously fought <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a><sup id="cite_ref-c795_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c795-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a><sup id="cite_ref-c928_9-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c928-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> and destroyed two ships belonging to <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c651_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c651-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> Kid rarely backs down from a battle and may fight a powerful enemy until his last breath. The fact that he did not join the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a> despite not standing a chance against Kaidou is a testament to Kid's disposition.<sup id="cite_ref-c954_12-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c954-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> Kid seems to believe that possessing the determination to achieve the impossible is necessary to survive in the New World, and that anyone who does not is as good as dead.<sup id="cite_ref-c594_21-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c594-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>Kid is very prideful of his reputation and aims to reach a top spot in the world of piracy, which he plans to achieve by beating the Four Emperors, even if it means dying for it.<sup id="cite_ref-c1029b_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1029b-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> That said, Kid has no interest in utilizing weapons of mass destruction (although he is curious about their existence) or other tools that could help him achieve those goals, instead just preferring to confront them head on with his own power.<sup id="cite_ref-c674_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c674-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> Because of this, he dislikes joining forces with others and sharing his targets with them, thinking that they will just interfere in what should be his fight alone.<sup id="cite_ref-c1015_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1015-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> He also hates being the subject of false rumors that paint him in a negative light, being quick to clarify them if he overhears someone talking about him.<sup id="cite_ref-c928_9-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c928-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> Because of his pride, Kid is notorious for being unreasonably stubborn, unwilling to back down no matter how impossible the task is. Despite this stubbornness, Kid has shown moments of maturity, willing to put his pride aside to work with his fellow Worst Generation members in overthrowing the Emperors of the Sea.  
</p><p>Kid is shown to be quite cynical about the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>. He is not blind to the way the <a href="/wiki/World_Noble" title="World Noble">World Nobles</a> act, remarking that, compared to them, pirates are almost humane in nature and honest about their faults, unlike the Nobles that justify their abuses of power through ancestry.<sup id="cite_ref-c500_22-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c500-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> After <a href="/wiki/Camie" title="Camie">Camie</a> had been sold in the <a href="/wiki/Human_Auctioning_House" title="Human Auctioning House">Human Auctioning House</a> to <a href="/wiki/Charlos" title="Charlos">Charlos</a>, Kid declared that the whole affair was a "farce"<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> and similarly held a similar point of view regarding the broadcast of the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Summit War of Marineford</a>, calling it a "charade".<sup id="cite_ref-c565_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c565-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> For this reason, he felt amusement and catharsis when the world noble <a href="/wiki/Charlos" title="Charlos">Charlos</a> was punched down by an irate <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">

  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">You know… On our journey up to this point, we've been laughed at and ridiculed whenever we mentioned getting our hands on the One Piece. And each time that happened, I slaughtered everyone who laughed. But what lies ahead is a sea of death for those who don't got the guts to mention it. Let's meet again in the New World!</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>

  </td>
 </tr>

<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f9/Luffy_And_Eustass_Kid.png/revision/latest?cb=20230809021715" class="image"><img alt="Luffy And Eustass Kid" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Luffy And Eustass Kid.png" data-image-key="Luffy_And_Eustass_Kid.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f9/Luffy_And_Eustass_Kid.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230809021715" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f9/Luffy_And_Eustass_Kid.png/revision/latest?cb=20230809021715" class="image"><img alt="Luffy And Eustass Kid" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f9/Luffy_And_Eustass_Kid.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230809021715" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Luffy And Eustass Kid.png" data-image-key="Luffy_And_Eustass_Kid.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f9/Luffy_And_Eustass_Kid.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230809021715" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Luffy_And_Eustass_Kid.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kid and Luffy display many similarities in terms of attitude.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kid has the same dream as <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a>: to find <a href="/wiki/One_Piece" title="One Piece">One Piece</a> and become the new Pirate King. Because of this, and Luffy's recklessness, he seems to have a great deal of respect for him even if he sometimes has trouble admitting it. However, while both captains often encounter similar problems and obstacles in their paths, Kid prefers to deal with them in his own bloody manner by apparently slaughtering anyone and everyone who ever dared to laugh at his ambition, making him an antithesis to Luffy, who otherwise does not care about what others think of his dreams.<sup id="cite_ref-c505p12_32-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c505p12-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c498p19_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c498p19-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> Surprisingly, belying his rough attitude, Kid can be childishly competitive and will mock his rivals any chance he gets, especially when Luffy and <a href="/wiki/Trafalgar_D._Water_Law" title="Trafalgar D. Water Law">Law</a> are involved.
</p><p>Another similarity Kid has to Luffy is a strong degree of affection for his crewmates. Kid will recklessly defend or rescue his subordinates if they are mocked or in danger. His concern for his longtime friend and right-hand man Killer having eaten a <a href="/wiki/SMILE" title="SMILE">SMILE</a> was enough that Kid did not care whatsoever about being captured a second time just a few days after managing to escape his captors.<sup id="cite_ref-c944_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c944-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> Kid is also rather gluttonous, not minding hard labor as long as he gets access to large amounts of food.<sup id="cite_ref-c926_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c926-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Unlike Luffy, however, Kid is rather unfriendly and mistrusting of others, rarely leaving his guard down and warning his subordinates to follow suit. The failure of his alliance with the <a href="/wiki/On_Air_Pirates" title="On Air Pirates">On Air Pirates</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hawkins_Pirates" title="Hawkins Pirates">Hawkins Pirates</a>, which happened due to the betrayal of <a href="/wiki/Scratchmen_Apoo" title="Scratchmen Apoo">Scratchmen Apoo</a>, seems to have reinforced this mindset, as he initially turned down an offer from Luffy to team up with the <a href="/wiki/Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai_Alliance" title="Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance">Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c950_20-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c950-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> Kid would eventually change his mind, but still acted as a reluctant ally for the most part, only joining forces with Luffy for the sake of their rivalry. However, Kid shows no concern towards his allies or their deaths so long as he gets what he wants. This turns out to be a flaw of Kid, as during his rematch against Shanks and his fleet, Kid approached his fleet without any allies around to help him and it costs him and his crew their ship and their Road Ponyglyph rubbings because of his pride. 
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Crew">Crew</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Kid seems to have a good relationship with his crewmembers that have been revealed. <a href="/wiki/Killer" title="Killer">Killer</a> keeps his captain calm when he gets angered. <a href="/wiki/Wire" title="Wire">Wire</a> and <a href="/wiki/Heat" title="Heat">Heat</a> hold high respect and concern for their captain. According to <a href="/wiki/Basil_Hawkins" title="Basil Hawkins">Basil Hawkins</a>, Kid's crew was forced to work under the <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Family" title="Kurozumi Family">Kurozumi Family</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a>, with the life of their captain being used as a bargaining chip.<sup id="cite_ref-c954_12-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c954-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After becoming Kaidou's prisoner, Kid was noticeably worried about what had happened to his crew and tried looking for them around the first time he escaped from the <a href="/wiki/Prisoner_Mine" title="Prisoner Mine">Prisoner Mine</a> at <a href="/wiki/Udon" title="Udon">Udon</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c944_33-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c944-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> Once he was freed for the second time thanks to Luffy's efforts, he still prioritized finding the rest of his crewmates and stated that he would only trust them from now on, as a result of Apoo and Hawkins' betrayal.
</p><p>During the <a href="/wiki/Raid_on_Onigashima" title="Raid on Onigashima">raid on Onigashima</a>, Kid's crew valiantly attempted to stand against Big Mom when the latter had seemingly managed to knock out their captain, although Kid eventually managed to recover and counterattack, to their delight. They also tearfully celebrated their boss's win against Big Mom and kept loyally protecting him even when it seemed like Kaidou had gained the upper hand over the alliance.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Killer">Killer</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Both Kid and Killer grew up together, so they share a close bond that goes back to childhood.<sup id="cite_ref-sbs87_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs87-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> Kid refers to Killer as his partner and is aware that the latter is sensitive about his own strange laugh, which is why, despite being unaware about Killer having eaten a defective <a href="/wiki/SMILE" title="SMILE">SMILE</a>, he knew something was wrong with his subordinate. This was enough for Kid to attempt a reckless rescue of his friend, which led to his second capture from the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a> after managing to escape the first time.<sup id="cite_ref-c944_33-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c944-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Killer has displayed immense loyalty for Kid multiple times; it was due to Kid's life being in danger that Killer ate a defective SMILE fruit and became a subordinate of <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Orochi" title="Kurozumi Orochi">Kurozumi Orochi</a>, showcasing extreme loyalty for Kid.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> Another notable instance of this happened during the war against the Beasts Pirates at <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a>, when Hawkins managed to link his life to Kid's, which forced Killer on the defensive so he would not accidentally kill his captain, even begging Hawkins to take his life instead as long as he left Kid's alone.
</p><p>Killer usually acts as the voice of reason for his captain, making sure Kid stays focused and does not lose sight of his goals due to impulsiveness.<sup id="cite_ref-c677_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c677-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> Killer also provides Kid with useful information whenever the latter displays curiosity in a certain topic.<sup id="cite_ref-c594_21-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c594-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Rivals">Rivals</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D10&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>As a member of the Worst Generation, he sees the other <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>100,000,000+ bounty rookies he encountered in the Sabaody Archipelago as his rivals, specifically Law and Luffy.<sup id="cite_ref-c505p12_32-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c505p12-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Monkey_D._Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D11&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">He gets on my nerves!</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:&#39;Arial&#39;,sans-serif;">—&#160;Kid after reading the article concerning Luffy's second visit to Marineford.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p><br />
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d1/Luffy_and_Kid_in_Udon_Prison.png/revision/latest?cb=20230302173705" class="image"><img alt="Luffy and Kid in Udon Prison" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="152" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Luffy and Kid in Udon Prison.png" data-image-key="Luffy_and_Kid_in_Udon_Prison.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d1/Luffy_and_Kid_in_Udon_Prison.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230302173705" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d1/Luffy_and_Kid_in_Udon_Prison.png/revision/latest?cb=20230302173705" class="image"><img alt="Luffy and Kid in Udon Prison" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d1/Luffy_and_Kid_in_Udon_Prison.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230302173705" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="152" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Luffy and Kid in Udon Prison.png" data-image-key="Luffy_and_Kid_in_Udon_Prison.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d1/Luffy_and_Kid_in_Udon_Prison.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230302173705" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Luffy_and_Kid_in_Udon_Prison.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Luffy and Kid compete by trying to carry more blocks than the other in Udon Prison.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kid sees <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a> as a prominent rival for the mantle of the next Pirate King, once declaring that they would become enemies in the <a href="/wiki/New_World" title="New World">New World</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c505p12_32-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c505p12-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> After the Whitebeard War, he stated that he was not generous enough to let Luffy run around as he pleased, showing intent to compete with him for notoriety and not get left behind. Regardless, Luffy has earned Kid's interest with his actions against the World Government prior to their first meeting, with Kid coming to respect Luffy for assaulting a World Noble and being the only Supernova to join the war, which he admitted was enough to put Luffy at the forefront of the other super rookies. After the timeskip, he expressed amusement when watching Luffy's capture on <a href="/wiki/Punk_Hazard" title="Punk Hazard">Punk Hazard</a> and, later, demonstrated great curiosity about the Luffy-Law alliance and their goals.<sup id="cite_ref-c677p3_6-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c677p3-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/70/Luffy_And_Kid_Fight_Dobon.png/revision/latest?cb=20200126120704" class="image"><img alt="Luffy And Kid Fight Dobon" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Luffy And Kid Fight Dobon.png" data-image-key="Luffy_And_Kid_Fight_Dobon.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/70/Luffy_And_Kid_Fight_Dobon.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20200126120704" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/70/Luffy_And_Kid_Fight_Dobon.png/revision/latest?cb=20200126120704" class="image"><img alt="Luffy And Kid Fight Dobon" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/70/Luffy_And_Kid_Fight_Dobon.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20200126120704" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Luffy And Kid Fight Dobon.png" data-image-key="Luffy_And_Kid_Fight_Dobon.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/70/Luffy_And_Kid_Fight_Dobon.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20200126120704" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Luffy_And_Kid_Fight_Dobon.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kid and Luffy team up againt Dobon.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After meeting again in a prison at Wano Country, Kid and Luffy became competitive with each other and would argue on about who had done more slave work. Despite this rivalry, they cooperated to defeat the deputy warden <a href="/wiki/Dobon" title="Dobon">Dobon</a> after he had confronted and tried to punish them for taking most of the prison's rations.<sup id="cite_ref-c926_34-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c926-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> Luffy also showed some concern for Kid when Queen threatened to drown him. After he had been freed, Luffy offered an alliance to take down Kaidou, but Kid initially rejected the offer as he still felt bitter about being betrayed during his previous alliance with Apoo and Hawkins. However, he joined Luffy and Law in the battle against the Beasts Pirates, not wanting Luffy to get all the glory in defeating Kaidou. Afterwards, despite his bounty increase, Kid's rivalry and general resentment with Luffy remained strong, with him angrily threatening Luffy with death for the latter's new spot in the <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Four Emperors</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> When leaving Wano, Kid provoked Luffy into racing him down at the waterfall.
</p><p>Despite frequent denials about viewing Luffy as an ally,<sup id="cite_ref-c1014_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1014-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> Kid seemingly trusts the Straw Hat captain's strength. While battling Big Mom by his lone self, Kid was visibly pleased upon learning that Luffy, even while knocked out, would not give up until he won against Kaidou, in spite of previous announcements that claimed he had died in combat against the Emperor. Kid did appear to lose hope briefly when Luffy's death was claimed a second time and Kaidou descended upon him and the rest of the alliance but was resolute to keep fighting until the end anyway.
</p><p>Kid calls Luffy "stupid monkey", while Luffy calls Kid "Jaggy"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">ギザ男</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Giza-o</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Trafalgar_D._Water_Law">Trafalgar D. Water Law</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D12&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">...I've heard rumors about him, and they weren't pleasant. His manners aren't too good either...</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:&#39;Arial&#39;,sans-serif;">—&#160;Kid about Law.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p>In the manga, <a href="/wiki/Trafalgar_D._Water_Law" title="Trafalgar D. Water Law">Law</a> gave Kid the finger when he (presumably) overheard Kid talking behind his back regarding rumors of how Law's manners appear to be rather lacking.<sup id="cite_ref-c500_22-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c500-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> Later on, when Kid volunteered to deal with the Marines amassing outside of the Auctioning House as a farewell gift to the Straw Hats and the Heart Pirates, both Law and Luffy took Kid's cockiness as an insult and opted to follow him outside in order to compete with the fellow super rookie. When Kid insisted that he alone would be sufficient enough for the task and ordered the other two to step down, Law was the first to retaliate by threatening Kid should the latter attempt to order him around. Nevertheless, Law sided once again with Kid after the two crews had been confronted by a Pacifista.
</p><p>Kid seems to have retained an interest in Law in the New World and was pleased to see that the surgeon was planning something instead of acting like a "Government Dog", further confirmed by his major interest in the Luffy-Law alliance. Later on, he teamed up with Law during the <a href="/wiki/Fire_Festival" title="Fire Festival">Fire Festival</a>, though they were still prone to arguing with each other.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> Kid seems to like mocking Law for his alliance with Luffy, especially since Law often follows Luffy's words.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> That said, he is annoyed when Law attempts to do the same to him by telling what to do.
</p><p>During the events of the <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country_Arc" title="Wano Country Arc">Wano Country Arc</a>, they teamed up together once more during the fight against Kaidou and Big Mom, even forming a brief alliance to take down the latter by herself. Despite Kid's protests about Law seemingly getting in his way and their general bickering over trivial things, he was able to work alongside the Surgeon of Death to defeat the Emperor. After Kaidou and Big Mom's downfalls, Law gives Kid another copy of <a href="/wiki/Poneglyph" title="Poneglyph">Road Poneglyph</a> for helping him and Luffy to defeat Kaidou and Big Mom. While leaving Wano, Kid provoked Law into racing down at the waterfall. 
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Enemies">Enemies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D13&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="World_Government">World Government</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D14&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">World Nobles... Slaves... Human shops... Against the "purity" of these "upper classes", the villains of the world look positively humane in comparison. It's because the world's in the hands of scum like them that it's all screwed to hell... I mean, we're not the nicest of guys, but at least we're honest about it.</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:&#39;Arial&#39;,sans-serif;">—&#160;Kid, commenting on the World Nobles.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p><br />
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7b/Law%2C_Kid_and_Luffy.png/revision/latest?cb=20210106140911" class="image"><img alt="Law, Kid and Luffy" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Law, Kid and Luffy.png" data-image-key="Law%2C_Kid_and_Luffy.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7b/Law%2C_Kid_and_Luffy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210106140911" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7b/Law%2C_Kid_and_Luffy.png/revision/latest?cb=20210106140911" class="image"><img alt="Law, Kid and Luffy" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7b/Law%2C_Kid_and_Luffy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210106140911" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Law, Kid and Luffy.png" data-image-key="Law%2C_Kid_and_Luffy.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7b/Law%2C_Kid_and_Luffy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210106140911" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Law,_Kid_and_Luffy.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kid, Luffy and Law standing against the Marines in front of the Human Auctioning House.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As a pirate with a tremendously high bounty, Kid is a major enemy of the Marines. Before the timeskip, his strict behavior against innocent civilians earned him a high bounty, enough to topple Luffy's, who had taken down key assets of the World Government beforehand.<sup id="cite_ref-c498p19_14-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c498p19-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> He, along with Trafalgar Law and Monkey D. Luffy, fought against many marine units at the <a href="/wiki/Sabaody_Archipelago" title="Sabaody Archipelago">Sabaody Archipelago</a>, with their combined being acknowledged by many of the infantrymen there.
</p><p>Kid also despises the <a href="/wiki/World_Noble" title="World Noble">World Nobles</a> and their actions, finding the notion that they can just own whoever they wanted due to their untouchable status as "farce". Apparently, Kid became a pirate himself with the intent of rebelling against what he considered the "scum" who ruled the world.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> Luffy showing up and punching <a href="/wiki/Charlos" title="Charlos">Charlos</a> in the face at the <a href="/wiki/Human_Auctioning_House" title="Human Auctioning House">Human Auctioning House</a> was met with much amusement from his part for that reason.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Four_Emperors">Four Emperors</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D15&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>According to Killer and Hawkins, Kid aims to hunt down the Four Emperors.<sup id="cite_ref-c1029b_26-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1029b-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> Kid has confronted many of them during his career, with varying degrees of success. After the events of the <a href="/wiki/Raid_on_Onigashima" title="Raid on Onigashima">raid on Onigashima</a>, Kid seemingly expected to become an Emperor himself, and was furious to find out he had been snubbed of the position despite his role in taking down Big Mom, overlooking the fact he needed Laws assistance to win.<sup id="cite_ref-c1053_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1053-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Shanks">Shanks</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D16&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>No direct interaction has been shown between the two, but Kid formed an alliance with fellow captains <a href="/wiki/Basil_Hawkins" title="Basil Hawkins">Basil Hawkins</a> and <a href="/wiki/Scratchmen_Apoo" title="Scratchmen Apoo">Scratchmen Apoo</a> to overthrow the Emperor, <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Red-Haired Shanks</a>. Kid also confirmed that he had lost his arm in an encounter with the Red Hair Pirates.<sup id="cite_ref-c928_9-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c928-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-sbs107_16-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs107-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>When Kid was later confronted into a battle with Shanks on Elbaph, he was excited at the possibility of battling Shanks for revenge for his prior loss despite the high probability of dying in the process, not showing any fear of losing.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> When he is forced to face off against Shanks' subordinate crew, Kid tries to destroy them all with his railgun, but he is instantly defeated by Shanks himself, who foresaw how catastrophic Kid's attack would be. Afterwards, Shanks' friends <a href="/wiki/Dorry" title="Dorry">Dorry</a> and <a href="/wiki/Brogy" title="Brogy">Brogy</a> destroyed his ship, knocking him and his entire crew into the sea and took his Poneglyph rubbings for himself.<sup id="cite_ref-c1079_13-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1079-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Charlotte_Linlin">Charlotte Linlin</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D17&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">You think the last gasps... of an old windbag scares me?!</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:&#39;Arial&#39;,sans-serif;">—&#160;Kid to Big Mom when he is immune to Soul Pocus.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p>During the timeskip, Kid invaded <a href="/wiki/Totto_Land" title="Totto Land">Totto Land</a> and injured one of <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a>'s Sweet Commanders before stealing a <a href="/wiki/Poneglyph" title="Poneglyph">poneglyph</a> rubbing from the Emperor. He later sunk two of the Emperor's ships while having no concern if she retaliated. Despite this hostility, Kid stated to <a href="/wiki/Caribou" title="Caribou">Caribou</a> that he had no interest in going after Big Mom.
</p><p>Kid met Big Mom again at Onigashima, with Kid taking part in the group who faced the duo of Kaidou and Big Mom at the top of the <a href="/wiki/Skull_Dome" title="Skull Dome">Skull Dome</a>. Kid was one of the Supernovas responsible for pushing Big Mom out of the Skull Dome's rooftop, which caused her to nearly drown into <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano Country</a>'s sea. When Big Mom made her way back into Onigashima, she specifically targeted Kid with her new homie <a href="/wiki/Hera" title="Hera">Hera</a> and angrily called out for him to reveal himself at her, still visibly furious about the stunt he had pulled that almost killed her.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> Kid, however, was not intimidated by her surprising return and kept hunting her down, intent on not letting her rejoin Kaidou. Kid somewhat regained his interest of taking down Big Mom just to get amount of fame. Kid declared to Big Mom that she is a nuisance when there is no place for her in the new era, in addition to calling her an "old-time pirate", much to Big Mom's rage.
</p><p>Big Mom seemingly did not take Kid seriously until he and Law managed to <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit#Awakening" title="Devil Fruit">severely injure</a> her. The resulting damage was enough to impress the Emperor, who then started to acknowledge their threat, even going as far as sacrificing some of her own life to gain additional power so she could crush the two. In the end, however, Big Mom's efforts were still not enough to take down Kid and Law, who both showed no fear at all towards her status as one of the Emperors, meaning they were immune to her <b><a href="/wiki/Soru_Soru_no_Mi#Techniques_2" title="Soru Soru no Mi">Soul Pocus</a></b> as well for Kid of calling Big Mom as an "old hag". Once Kid and Law managed to launch her down into a crater with the help of an explosive she accidentally detonated, Big Mom, confident that she would not die, swore that they would pay.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Kaidou">Kaidou</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D18&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Kid encountered <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a> when the latter fell out of the sky and landed at the Kid Pirates' hideout before coming face to face with the rookie pirate. Kid refused to submit to Kaidou and tried to fight him only to be defeated and captured. Kaidou then imprisoned Kid, hoping to eventually break his spirit and turn him into a soldier for the Beasts.
</p><p>During his imprisonment, Kid was shown to hold a strong grudge against Kaidou and firmly told Luffy that he would be the one to defeat the Emperor.<sup id="cite_ref-c928_9-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c928-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> However, after seeing what happened to Killer, Kid decided to prioritize finding the rest of his crew and rejected Luffy's offer for an alliance.
</p><p>After getting his crew back, he joined Luffy and Law to take down Kaidou, but just for the glory of defeating him and getting back for what the Beasts Pirates had done to him and his crew, not for the Kouzuki revolution. He took part in the confrontation against both Kaidou and Big Mom at the top of the Skull Dome.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Buggy">Buggy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D19&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Kid apparently does not take <a href="/wiki/Buggy" title="Buggy">Buggy</a> as an Emperor seriously, implying that he holds no respect for the clown pirate at all.
