Kid has even admitted that the notion of Buggy as an Emperor was worse for him to deal with than Luffy having the same status, although he did seem entertained at the idea behind the <a href="/wiki/Cross_Guild" title="Cross Guild">Cross Guild</a> and its capability of issuing bounties on the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c1056_47-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1056-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Scratchmen_Apoo">Scratchmen Apoo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D20&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Kid once got into a fight with <a href="/wiki/Scratchmen_Apoo" title="Scratchmen Apoo">Apoo</a> at <a href="/wiki/Sabaody_Archipelago" title="Sabaody Archipelago">Sabaody Archipelago</a>, but they both agreed to postpone their fight until after they had entered the New World. During their meeting in the <a href="/wiki/New_World" title="New World">New World</a>, Apoo wrecked Kid's hideout and beat up one of his crew members because of the possibility that Kid was hiding a sniper, enraging Kid and resulting in a scuffle. However, it was revealed shortly afterwards, they in fact planned to form an alliance.<sup id="cite_ref-c677_10-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c677-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> Despite their differences, they came into an agreement.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/33/Kid_confronts_Apoo.png/revision/latest?cb=20230625230415" class="image"><img alt="Kid confronts Apoo" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kid confronts Apoo.png" data-image-key="Kid_confronts_Apoo.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/33/Kid_confronts_Apoo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230625230415" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/33/Kid_confronts_Apoo.png/revision/latest?cb=20230625230415" class="image"><img alt="Kid confronts Apoo" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/33/Kid_confronts_Apoo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230625230415" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kid confronts Apoo.png" data-image-key="Kid_confronts_Apoo.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/33/Kid_confronts_Apoo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230625230415" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kid_confronts_Apoo.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kid confronting Apoo over his betrayal of their alliance.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kid and Apoo seemed to have gotten on more amiable terms with each other as themselves and their crews were able to eat and party together.<sup id="cite_ref-c793_48-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c793-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> However, following the encounter with Kaidou, Apoo revealed himself to be a spy for the Beasts Pirates, having already joined Kaidou beforehand and letting the Emperor know about the location of their <a href="/wiki/Pirate_Alliance" title="Pirate Alliance">Pirate Alliance</a>, leading to Kid distrusting other pirates except his own crew. Upon seeing Apoo again during the <a href="/wiki/Raid_on_Onigashima" title="Raid on Onigashima">raid on Onigashima</a>, Kid wasted no time attacking him, even disregarding the risk of revealing his presence to the Beasts Pirates. Apoo did not regret betraying Kid, as he himself looked down to the concept of alliances, thinking they never ended well.<sup id="cite_ref-c980_24-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c980-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Following the events of the raid on Onigashima, Kid and Apoo appear to have gone back to at least mildly tolerating each other, with Kid still disliking Apoo's presence, but not to the point of sheer hostility.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Basil_Hawkins">Basil Hawkins</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D21&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/Basil_Hawkins" title="Basil Hawkins">Hawkins</a> was another Worst Generation captain that Kid formed an alliance with, alongside Apoo. At first, Hawkins showed impatience regarding Kid and Apoo's animosity and nearly left the meeting but was convinced by Killer to stay.<sup id="cite_ref-c677_10-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c677-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> Kid and Hawkins eventually came into an agreement, with <a href="/wiki/Hawkins_Pirates" title="Hawkins Pirates">Hawkins' crew</a> later being shown partying with the Kid and <a href="/wiki/On_Air_Pirates" title="On Air Pirates">On Air Pirates</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c793_48-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c793-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>However, when Kaidou crashed into Kid's hideout and faced the alliance, Hawkins did not stand up against the Emperor and accepted to join the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a> out of survival. He did witness Kid and Killer fighting Kaidou to the end and was aware that Kid would not submit himself to anyone.<sup id="cite_ref-c954_12-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c954-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later at Onigashima, Hawkins confronted both Kid and Killer. Kid considered Hawkins a traitor, but the latter justified himself that he had been betrayed by Apoo as well and followed the only choice he had at the time.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> Unbeknownst to Kid, Hawkins had somehow managed to <a href="/wiki/Wara_Wara_no_Mi" title="Wara Wara no Mi">link his own life to his</a> at some point, which led to Kid being sabotaged as he fought Big Mom, something that greatly amused Hawkins. Ultimately, Killer fought Hawkins on his own and was able to defeat him on Kid's behalf.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later on, Hawkins admitted to <a href="/wiki/X_Drake" title="X Drake">X Drake</a> that, despite foreseeing Kaidou's downfall, he did not attempt to join forces with Kid again out of pride and shame for not opposing Kaidou the same way Kid did, confirming what Killer had told him earlier during their fight.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Abilities_and_Powers">Abilities and Powers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D22&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>As the captain of the <a href="/wiki/Kid_Pirates" title="Kid Pirates">Kid Pirates</a>, Kid has complete authority over the crew. As a member of the Worst Generation, he is a powerful pirate.
</p><p>Prior to the timeskip, he had a reward of <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>315,000,000, the highest among the Eleven Supernovas at the time, for dealing major destruction and civilian casualties along their route through the <a href="/wiki/Grand_Line" title="Grand Line">Grand Line</a> and towards the <a href="/wiki/New_World" title="New World">New World</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c498p19_14-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c498p19-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> In the <a href="/wiki/Human_Auctioning_House" title="Human Auctioning House">Human Auctioning House</a>, he effortlessly defeated a large group of <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a> alongside <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> and <a href="/wiki/Trafalgar_D._Water_Law" title="Trafalgar D. Water Law">Trafalgar Law</a>. Later, he along with his crew also managed to escape from a <a href="/wiki/Pacifista" title="Pacifista">Pacifista</a> and <a href="/wiki/Admiral" title="Admiral">Admiral</a> <a href="/wiki/Borsalino" title="Borsalino">Kizaru</a>.
</p><p>After the timeskip, Kid appears to have become much more powerful, surviving the <a href="/wiki/Red_Hair_Pirates" title="Red Hair Pirates">Red Hair Pirates</a> to a battle and wounding one of Big Mom's <a href="/wiki/Big_Mom_Pirates#Sweet_Commanders" title="Big Mom Pirates">Sweet Commanders</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-c928_9-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c928-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> as well as later destroying two ships belonging to her.<sup id="cite_ref-c651_25-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c651-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> His bounty rose to <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>470,000,000.<sup id="cite_ref-c677p3_6-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c677p3-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>During the <a href="/wiki/Raid_on_Onigashima" title="Raid on Onigashima">Raid on Onigashima</a>, he has shown to be powerful enough to fight against the two <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Emperors</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a> and Big Mom, dealing damage to them despite their near-impenetrable defenses.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> Later, Kid briefly faced Big Mom, in a singles match, before wrestling, alongside <a href="/wiki/Trafalgar_D._Water_Law" title="Trafalgar D. Water Law">Law</a>, in a match receiving <a href="/wiki/Basil_Hawkins" title="Basil Hawkins">Hawkins</a>' <a href="/wiki/Wara_Wara_no_Mi" title="Wara Wara no Mi">damage</a>. After she had been empowered with a year of her life, while wielding her special Homies, <a href="/wiki/Hera" title="Hera">Hera</a>, <a href="/wiki/Prometheus" title="Prometheus">Prometheus</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Napoleon" title="Napoleon">Napoleon</a>, all of whom had grown stronger and more in sync, the two <a href="/wiki/Super_Rookie" title="Super Rookie">Supernovas</a>, often using their awakened powers managed to push Big Mom towards her limits and landing a devastating blow against the feared Emperor, resulting in her eventual defeat.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>Having defeated the former Emperor, <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a>, Kid gained a bounty of <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>3,000,000,000,<sup id="cite_ref-c1053_5-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1053-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> making him one of the most dangerous pirates in the world, with his new bounty matching that of the current Emperor and rival, Monkey D Luffy. However, in spite of his increase in strength, he still is no match for an Emperor head on, having been easily defeated by Shanks alone due to having overestimated his own strength compared to the Emperor, a mistake that potentially cost him and his crew their lives. 
</p><p>Kid also appears well-connected, as he is aware of dealings within the <a href="/wiki/Broker" title="Broker">underworld</a> and knew about <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Clown" title="Caesar Clown">Caesar Clown</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Shinokuni" title="Shinokuni">experiments</a>.
</p><p>Additionally, Kid has a strong will, as he was completely unaffected by a burst of <a href="/wiki/Silvers_Rayleigh" title="Silvers Rayleigh">Rayleigh</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> Like <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a> and Law, Kid is also immune to Big Mom's "<a href="/wiki/Soru_Soru_no_Mi#Techniques_2" title="Soru Soru no Mi"><b>Soul Pocus</b></a>" due to his lack of fear towards the Emperor.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_Abilities">Physical Abilities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D23&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Kid possesses immense physical strength and resilience. While being cuffed with <a href="/wiki/Seastone" title="Seastone">Seastone</a>, which depletes the energy of <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> users, he was able to match Luffy's speed in carrying and delivering large stone blocks bigger than him even with only one arm. He was also able to endure the torture of his imprisonment by the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a>. More impressively, Kid has enough power to challenge and fight against two members of the <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Four Emperors</a> on the roof of Onigashima, withstand multiple attacks from both Emperors, and even deal damage to both Emperors who were both known for their near invulnerable bodies. Later inside of Onigashima, he was able to battle one of the Emperors head on, being able to withstand or even overpower direct attacks from the monstrously strong Big Mom, even after she had empowered herself further with her <a href="/wiki/Soru_Soru_no_Mi" title="Soru Soru no Mi">Devil Fruit abilities</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c1013_57-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1013-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> Another impressive feat was the fact that he was able to clash with her even while unknowingly under the effects of Basil Hawkins' <a href="/wiki/Wara_Wara_no_Mi" title="Wara Wara no Mi">Devil Fruit abilities</a>.
</p><p>Kid has an extraordinary recovery rate, as one of the prison guards said that his body could heal in a few days. Similar to Luffy, Kid has an incredible metabolism where he can eat large amounts of food, to the point where he becomes fat and round, but instantly burns all the calories to replenish his stamina.<sup id="cite_ref-c926_34-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c926-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Kid is also an extremely skilled hand-to-hand combatant. While bound by Seastone cuffs and with only one arm, he managed to defeat <a href="/wiki/Dobon" title="Dobon">Dobon</a>, a Shinuchi of the Beast Pirates, alongside Luffy. Kid also managed to escape the <a href="/wiki/Udon" title="Udon">Udon</a> <a href="/wiki/Prisoner_Mine" title="Prisoner Mine">Prisoner Mine</a>, while still cuffed in Seastone shackles.<sup id="cite_ref-c934_58-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c934-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Devil_Fruit">Devil Fruit</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D24&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Jiki_Jiki_no_Mi" title="Jiki Jiki no Mi">Jiki Jiki no Mi</a></i></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Magnetic_Iron_Claw.png/revision/latest?cb=20231216221243" class="image"><img alt="Magnetic Iron Claw" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Magnetic Iron Claw.png" data-image-key="Magnetic_Iron_Claw.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Magnetic_Iron_Claw.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231216221243" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Magnetic_Iron_Claw.png/revision/latest?cb=20231216221243" class="image"><img alt="Magnetic Iron Claw" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Magnetic_Iron_Claw.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231216221243" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Magnetic Iron Claw.png" data-image-key="Magnetic_Iron_Claw.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Magnetic_Iron_Claw.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231216221243" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Magnetic_Iron_Claw.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kid using his magnetism to form a giant hand out of scrap metal.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kid ate the Jiki Jiki no Mi, a <a href="/wiki/Paramecia" title="Paramecia">Paramecia</a>-type <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> that allows him to manipulate magnetic forces. He can attract and/or repel metal objects as he pleases, and he can also create magnetic fields that allow him to arrange metal objects into various configurations and constructs.
</p><p>Kid can arrange the metal objects stuck to his body into a variety of shapes, with his most common technique being to form a gigantic metal arm used to unleash powerful attacks. In addition to covering his real arms with metal, Kid was also shown using his magnetism to form a rough replacement left arm after his cybernetic left arm had been removed by the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c950_20-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c950-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>This power makes Kid a very dangerous opponent against fighters who use metal weapons, since he can either repel metal projectiles, such as cannonballs and bullets, or attract his enemies' blades and guns towards himself to use as building material for his own attacks.<sup id="cite_ref-c504_59-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c504-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Awakening">Awakening</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D25&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2a/Assign.png/revision/latest?cb=20230625131036" class="image"><img alt="Assign" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="189" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Assign.png" data-image-key="Assign.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2a/Assign.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230625131036" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2a/Assign.png/revision/latest?cb=20230625131036" class="image"><img alt="Assign" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2a/Assign.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230625131036" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="189" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Assign.png" data-image-key="Assign.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2a/Assign.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230625131036" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Assign.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kid using his awakening to magnetize Big Mom.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kid has achieved Devil Fruit <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit#Awakening" title="Devil Fruit">Awakening</a>, allowing him to bestow magnetic properties onto things other than his own body. By his own admission, he has not fully mastered his awakened powers and it takes a serious toll on his stamina.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup><br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Haki">Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D26&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Haki" title="Haki">Haki</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>Kid is one of the very few people in the world who can use all three types of Haki.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_3-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> Despite this, he rarely uses them in combat, being more reliant on his Devil Fruit abilities. 
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Supreme_King_Haki">Supreme King Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D27&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>According to Kaidou, Kid possesses the ability to use <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> a very rare form of Haki whose users are said to have the qualities of a "<a href="/wiki/King_(Title)" title="King (Title)">king</a>". While he has not yet showcased his usage of it in the manga, Kid has been seen using it in both the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_(Anime)" title="One Piece (Anime)">Anime</a><sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/One_Piece:_Pirate_Warriors_4" title="One Piece: Pirate Warriors 4">One Piece: Pirate Warriors 4</a>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Observation_Haki">Observation Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D28&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Kid is a very skilled user of <a href="/wiki/Haki/Observation_Haki" title="Haki/Observation Haki">Observation Haki</a>, which he showcased during the <a href="/wiki/Raid_on_Onigashima" title="Raid on Onigashima">Raid on Onigashima</a>. He was able to sense that Luffy was defeated by Kaidou,<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> and was also able to sense Luffy's <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_5_Techniques" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 5 Techniques">Devil Fruit Awakening</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Armament_Haki">Armament Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D29&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Kid possesses the ability to use <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Armament Haki</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_3-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>  
</p><p>Non-canonically, in <a href="/wiki/One_Piece:_Stampede" title="One Piece: Stampede">One Piece: Stampede</a> Kid showcases hardening both of his metal arms during his fight with <a href="/wiki/Douglas_Bullet" title="Douglas Bullet">Douglas Bullet</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-film14_65-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-film14-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> and in the anime he is seen hardening his arm and proceeds to then punch <a href="/wiki/Poker" title="Poker">Poker</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Weapons">Weapons</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D30&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Kid carries around a <a href="/wiki/Firearm" title="Firearm">flintlock pistol</a> and a dagger. Sometime during the timeskip, his left arm was replaced with a mechanical one, making him a <a href="/wiki/Cyborgs" title="Cyborgs">cyborg</a>.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D31&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Past">Past</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D32&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Kid was born in the <a href="/wiki/South_Blue" title="South Blue">South Blue</a> in an island unaffiliated with the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Past_67-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Past-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> He knew <a href="/wiki/Killer" title="Killer">Killer</a> since they were children. One day, they ate curry udon with their first love, <a href="/wiki/Victoria_Shiruton_Doruyanaika" title="Victoria Shiruton Doruyanaika">Victoria Shiruton Doruyanaika</a>. They laughed when she spilled curry broth all over herself while eating it, causing her to beat them up. This caused curry udon to become their least favorite food.<sup id="cite_ref-sbs87_35-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs87-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Kid, Killer, <a href="/wiki/Heat" title="Heat">Heat</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wire" title="Wire">Wire</a> were bosses of gangs ruling the island's four towns. After Victoria was murdered by a rival gang, Kid unified the four groups and took down the rival gang. He then decided to form <a href="/wiki/Kid_Pirates" title="Kid Pirates">a pirate crew</a>, naming their ship <a href="/wiki/Victoria_Punk" title="Victoria Punk">Victoria Punk</a> after Victoria, with Kid as the <a href="/wiki/Pirate_Captain" title="Pirate Captain">captain</a> and Killer as his right-hand man.<sup id="cite_ref-Past_67-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Past-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> They were noted to have been responsible for a great deal of damage and had caused many civilian casualties for the slightest provocations along their journey. By the time he was 19 years old, he had already achieved an infamous reputation, having been mentioned by <a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Ace" title="Portgas D. Ace">Portgas D. Ace</a> four years ago as having caused a significant impact in the sea.<sup id="cite_ref-c498p19_14-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c498p19-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>They eventually entered the <a href="/wiki/Grand_Line" title="Grand Line">Grand Line</a> in search of the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece" title="One Piece">One Piece</a>. After a long voyage following one of the <a href="/wiki/Log_Pose" title="Log Pose">Log Pose</a> routes of the Grand Line, Kid and his crew arrived at the <a href="/wiki/Sabaody_Archipelago" title="Sabaody Archipelago">Sabaody Archipelago</a> to prepare themselves for the <a href="/wiki/New_World" title="New World">New World</a>. By that time, Kid had earned himself a staggering bounty of <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>315,000,000, making him a member of the as-of-yet named <a href="/wiki/Worst_Generation" title="Worst Generation">Worst Generation</a> alongside Killer.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Summit_War_Saga">Summit War Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D33&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Sabaody_Archipelago_Arc">Sabaody Archipelago Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D34&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>While at the archipelago, he had a little squabble with <a href="/wiki/Scratchmen_Apoo" title="Scratchmen Apoo">Scratchmen Apoo</a> in Grove 24. Before their battle could escalate further, Apoo asked Kid to postpone it until they went to the New World. Knowing what would happen if an incident were to happen, Kid agreed to Apoo's terms.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Kid and his crew then ventured deeper into the mangrove and entered the <a href="/wiki/Human_Auctioning_House" title="Human Auctioning House">Human Auctioning House</a>. As Kid waited for the auction to begin, he made a number of remarks to his crew, claiming that the World Nobles make pirates seem humane by comparison and bemoaning the twisted nature of the world order, before noting that he might actually join in on the slave auction. Kid later caught a glimpse of <a href="/wiki/Trafalgar_D._Water_Law" title="Trafalgar D. Water Law">Trafalgar Law</a>, who was already sitting for the auction, and was flipped off by the pirate doctor.<sup id="cite_ref-c500_22-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c500-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> As the auction began, Kid noticed some members of the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> coming in and was disappointed to find the captain was not with them at the time, noting that he wished to see just how big an idiot and how crazy <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> is supposed to be, as depicted in the newspapers.
</p><p>Kid watched through most of the auction, until the <a href="/wiki/World_Noble" title="World Noble">World Noble</a> Saint <a href="/wiki/Charlos" title="Charlos">Charlos</a> made an outrageously high <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>500,000,000 bid for the <a href="/wiki/Merfolk" title="Merfolk">mermaid</a>, <a href="/wiki/Camie" title="Camie">Camie</a>, which completely shut out the other participants in the auction. Seeing the noble went unchallenged, Kid decided to leave the auction house, considering it another example of what is wrong with the world. However, before he and his crew left the building, Luffy and <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</a> crashed through the wall right next to them. What followed next then was a ruckus caused by Luffy that caught Kid's eye. As the events unraveled, Kid, along with the rest of the crowd, watched in shock as Luffy punched Charlos out of anger for shooting his <a href="/wiki/Fish-Men" title="Fish-Men">fish-man</a> ally, <a href="/wiki/Hatchan" title="Hatchan">Hatchan</a>. While most of everyone in the auction house started panicking at this turn of events, Kid, as well as Trafalgar Law, simply smiled approvingly at what happened.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Just as Kid was watching the ensuing chaos, he noticed that someone suddenly came out of the back of the auction house's stage, along with a giant. He then witnessed the person knocking out nearly everyone in the place except for the Straw Hats and their allies with <a href="/wiki/Haki" title="Haki">Haki</a>. Having taken the blast and survived through it, Kid realized that this person was none other than <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a>'s first mate, <a href="/wiki/Silvers_Rayleigh" title="Silvers Rayleigh">Silvers Rayleigh</a>. As the situation continued, Kid and those still conscious realized that a bunch of <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a> were surrounding the auction house for what Luffy did.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/37/Pirate_Captain.png/revision/latest?cb=20230330171408" class="image"><img alt="Pirate Captain" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="149" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Pirate Captain.png" data-image-key="Pirate_Captain.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/37/Pirate_Captain.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230330171408" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/37/Pirate_Captain.png/revision/latest?cb=20230330171408" class="image"><img alt="Pirate Captain" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/37/Pirate_Captain.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230330171408" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="149" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Pirate Captain.png" data-image-key="Pirate_Captain.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/37/Pirate_Captain.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230330171408" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Pirate_Captain.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kid, Luffy and Law confront the Marines.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Though happy at seeing how crazy Luffy is as the rumors stated, Kid decided not to stick around to fight a Marine Admiral. Seeing as how the Marines were treating Kid's and <a href="/wiki/Heart_Pirates" title="Heart Pirates">Law's crews</a> as if they were accomplices to the Straw Hats, Kid told Luffy and Law that he would go on ahead and clear a way for them so that they would not have to worry themselves. However, Luffy and Law were insulted by Kid's remarks, and instead decided to go face the Marines along with him. Together, the three captains began to fight the Marines outside the auction house with their respective <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> powers.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> Luffy noted that both Kid and Law have crazy powers, with Kid responding that Luffy had the weirdest.
</p><p>After beating back, the first wave of Marine attacks and scattering them, Kid noted that their plan of attack was utterly demolished. He bid Luffy farewell and stated that it was nice meeting him, but promised that the next time they meet, he would not be so merciful. Luffy unconcernedly replied that he would be the one to find <a href="/wiki/One_Piece" title="One Piece">One Piece</a>. Both Kid and Law stared at Luffy and were even distracted from the attacking Marines. <a href="/wiki/Killer" title="Killer">Killer</a> defended Kid and scolded him for not paying attention. Kid reflected to Luffy that on his voyage, people had laughed when he made the same claim and he killed everyone who laughed at him. He also stated that from this point, anyone without the nerve to claim One Piece would die on the seas. He invited both Luffy and Law to meet up with him in the New World before departing with his crew.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d8/Heart_and_Kid_Pirates_vs._Pacifista.png/revision/latest?cb=20230330171625" class="image"><img alt="Heart and Kid Pirates vs" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="120" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Heart and Kid Pirates vs. Pacifista.png" data-image-key="Heart_and_Kid_Pirates_vs._Pacifista.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d8/Heart_and_Kid_Pirates_vs._Pacifista.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230330171625" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d8/Heart_and_Kid_Pirates_vs._Pacifista.png/revision/latest?cb=20230330171625" class="image"><img alt="Heart and Kid Pirates vs" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d8/Heart_and_Kid_Pirates_vs._Pacifista.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230330171625" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="120" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Heart and Kid Pirates vs. Pacifista.png" data-image-key="Heart_and_Kid_Pirates_vs._Pacifista.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d8/Heart_and_Kid_Pirates_vs._Pacifista.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230330171625" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Heart_and_Kid_Pirates_vs._Pacifista.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kid and Law confronting a Pacifista.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After defeating the Marines, the Kid Pirates were on their way to leave the island when moments later, Kid and his crew were confronted by what they believed to be <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Warlord of the Sea</a> <a href="/wiki/Bartholomew_Kuma" title="Bartholomew Kuma">Bartholomew Kuma</a> (later revealed to be a <a href="/wiki/Pacifista" title="Pacifista">Pacifista</a>). It surprised both Kid and the pirates when it fired a laser from its mouth which hit Kid's left leg.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup> Law and his crew happened to encounter them while escaping as well and, despite Kid telling Law to stay back (which is met once again by Law's earlier threat), they both prepared to fight against the Pacifista.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Marineford_Arc">Marineford Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D35&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Kid and his crew managed to escape capture by the Pacifista and later returned to Sabaody Archipelago. They watched the live broadcast of the execution of <a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Ace" title="Portgas D. Ace">Portgas D. Ace</a> up until it was cut off by the Marines. After this, Kid told his men they were departing.<sup id="cite_ref-c565_30-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c565-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Post-War_Arc">Post-War Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D36&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>The Kid Pirates then approached <a href="/wiki/Marineford" title="Marineford">Marineford</a> and watched the war unfold from a safe distance on board of their ship. After the war was declared over by <a href="/wiki/Sengoku" title="Sengoku">Sengoku</a>, Kid commented that since <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a> died, the balance of the <a href="/wiki/Three_Great_Powers" title="Three Great Powers">Three Great Powers</a> was shifted with the New World under the control of the remaining <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Emperors</a> <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a>. Kid went on saying that the New Age, the likes of which no one has ever seen before, had begun.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6c/Eustass_Kid_in_the_New_World.png/revision/latest?cb=20210912033525" class="image"><img alt="Eustass Kid in the New World" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Eustass Kid in the New World.png" data-image-key="Eustass_Kid_in_the_New_World.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6c/Eustass_Kid_in_the_New_World.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210912033525" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6c/Eustass_Kid_in_the_New_World.png/revision/latest?cb=20210912033525" class="image"><img alt="Eustass Kid in the New World" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6c/Eustass_Kid_in_the_New_World.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210912033525" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Eustass Kid in the New World.png" data-image-key="Eustass_Kid_in_the_New_World.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6c/Eustass_Kid_in_the_New_World.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210912033525" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Eustass_Kid_in_the_New_World.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kid crucifying a defeated pirate crew.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kid and his crew later arrived in the New World. He was reading aloud from the newspaper article about Luffy going to Marineford a second time. Following Killer's explanation about the <a href="/wiki/Ox_Bell" title="Ox Bell">Ox Bell</a>, Kid thought Luffy's message meant a declaration of creating the new age himself. Kid found this amusing and acknowledged Luffy's boldness, but, at the same time, he was not generous enough to let Luffy stay ahead of him much longer. He then took <a href="/wiki/Haritsu_Kendiyo" title="Haritsu Kendiyo">Haritsu Kendiyo</a> and his pirate crew captive and crucified them using his Devil Fruit powers despite their pleas for mercy, saying that people with that little amount of resolve had no business in the New World.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="During_the_Timeskip">During the Timeskip</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D37&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Sometime during the two-year timeskip, as Kid got very involved in many conflicts,<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_3-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> he lost his left forearm in battle against the <a href="/wiki/Red_Hair_Pirates" title="Red Hair Pirates">Red Hair Pirates</a> first mate <a href="/wiki/Benn_Beckman" title="Benn Beckman">Benn Beckman</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-sbs107_16-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs107-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c928_9-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c928-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> He later replaced it with a large metal one.<sup id="cite_ref-c677p3_6-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c677p3-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> Furthermore, his bounty has increased to <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>470,000,000.<sup id="cite_ref-c677p3_6-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c677p3-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>At some point after this, Kid and his crew went to Big Mom's <a href="/wiki/Totto_Land" title="Totto Land">territory</a> and injured one of Big Mom's <a href="/wiki/Big_Mom_Pirates#Three_Sweet_Commanders" title="Big Mom Pirates">Sweet Commanders</a>, as well as plundering a copy of her Road Poneglyph.<sup id="cite_ref-c928_9-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c928-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> However, they were quickly forced to flee afterwards.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Dressrosa_Saga">Dressrosa Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D38&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Punk_Hazard_Arc">Punk Hazard Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D39&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/50/Kid_Watches_Broadcast.png/revision/latest?cb=20130625024243" class="image"><img alt="Kid Watches Broadcast" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="190" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kid Watches Broadcast.png" data-image-key="Kid_Watches_Broadcast.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/50/Kid_Watches_Broadcast.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20130625024243" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/50/Kid_Watches_Broadcast.png/revision/latest?cb=20130625024243" class="image"><img alt="Kid Watches Broadcast" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/50/Kid_Watches_Broadcast.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20130625024243" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="190" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kid Watches Broadcast.png" data-image-key="Kid_Watches_Broadcast.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/50/Kid_Watches_Broadcast.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20130625024243" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kid_Watches_Broadcast.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kid watching the Punk Hazard broadcast.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>A few days after sinking two of the Big Mom Pirates' ships,<sup id="cite_ref-c651_25-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c651-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> Kid watched <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Clown" title="Caesar Clown">Caesar Clown</a>'s broadcast of his new <a href="/wiki/Smiley" title="Smiley">weapon of mass destruction</a> via a video <a href="/wiki/Den_Den_Mushi" title="Den Den Mushi">Den Den Mushi</a>. When asked by Killer if he was interested in purchasing said weapon, he denied it, simply wanting to satisfy his curiosity about news on the black market despite his unaffiliation with <a href="/wiki/Broker" title="Broker">broker</a> activities.<sup id="cite_ref-c674_27-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c674-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>After seeing his fellow Supernovas Luffy and Law captured, Kid then left the broadcast at the urging of Killer to meet up with some apparent guests they had summoned beforehand. Kid also mentioned that he was surprised about how Law was really planning something all along, having believed he had become a mere <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">government dog</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c677_10-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c677-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1b/Kid%2C_Hawkins%2C_and_Apoo_Meeting.png/revision/latest?cb=20230626000750" class="image"><img alt="Kid, Hawkins, and Apoo Meeting" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kid, Hawkins, and Apoo Meeting.png" data-image-key="Kid%2C_Hawkins%2C_and_Apoo_Meeting.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1b/Kid%2C_Hawkins%2C_and_Apoo_Meeting.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230626000750" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1b/Kid%2C_Hawkins%2C_and_Apoo_Meeting.png/revision/latest?cb=20230626000750" class="image"><img alt="Kid, Hawkins, and Apoo Meeting" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1b/Kid%2C_Hawkins%2C_and_Apoo_Meeting.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230626000750" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kid, Hawkins, and Apoo Meeting.png" data-image-key="Kid%2C_Hawkins%2C_and_Apoo_Meeting.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1b/Kid%2C_Hawkins%2C_and_Apoo_Meeting.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230626000750" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kid,_Hawkins,_and_Apoo_Meeting.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kid, Apoo and Hawkins meeting in the New World.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Opening the door to the meeting room of his hideout, it was revealed that the guests were none other than Scratchmen Apoo and <a href="/wiki/Basil_Hawkins" title="Basil Hawkins">Basil Hawkins</a>. Apoo, standing amongst a wrecked room and over one of Kid's badly beaten subordinates, started taunting Kid, leading him to instantly become enraged at the Longarm due to the damage he had caused. As the two challenged each other, Hawkins declared how foolish the meeting was and that he was leaving. Killer asked him to wait as he stepped between Kid and Apoo, reminding them that the three crews came together to try and form an alliance and asked that they at least try to discuss it.<sup id="cite_ref-c677_10-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c677-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>A newspaper later revealed that the three captains came to an agreement and formed an alliance.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Dressrosa_Arc">Dressrosa Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D40&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After reading the <a href="/wiki/Newspaper" title="Newspaper">newspaper</a>, he saw that Luffy, and Law had formed their own alliance and wondered which <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Emperor</a> they were targeting.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Kid, Hawkins, and Apoo were dining together when they heard the news of <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Doflamingo" title="Donquixote Doflamingo">Donquixote Doflamingo</a>'s defeat. They figured that Luffy, and Law were after Kaidou since Doflamingo was connected to him. They were pleased that Luffy and Law were not after the same Emperor as them, <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c793_48-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c793-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6c/Kid_Pirates_Face_Kaidou.png/revision/latest?cb=20210107064548" class="image"><img alt="Kid Pirates Face Kaidou" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kid Pirates Face Kaidou.png" data-image-key="Kid_Pirates_Face_Kaidou.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6c/Kid_Pirates_Face_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210107064548" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6c/Kid_Pirates_Face_Kaidou.png/revision/latest?cb=20210107064548" class="image"><img alt="Kid Pirates Face Kaidou" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6c/Kid_Pirates_Face_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210107064548" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kid Pirates Face Kaidou.png" data-image-key="Kid_Pirates_Face_Kaidou.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6c/Kid_Pirates_Face_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210107064548" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kid_Pirates_Face_Kaidou.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kid finds himself facing Kaidou.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Sometime later, Kid and the others were alerted by what seemed to be an earthquake. Kid instructed his men to have their weapons drawn and drew closer to investigate. The source of the commotion was a large crater on the ground in the shape of a human. Kid was enraged and demanded an answer as to what person was behind this occurrence. He was answered by another explosion in the direction of the crater. It was then revealed that the man who had caused the explosion was Kaidou.<sup id="cite_ref-c795_11-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c795-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> At that time, Kid, Killer, and Hawkins discovered that Apoo was already working for Kaidou with the intention of setting them up to join him as his subordinates. While Hawkins joined Kaidou, Kid and Killer refused to submit to the Emperor and tried to fight him, only to be defeated.<sup id="cite_ref-c954_12-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c954-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup><br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Whole_Cake_Island_Saga">Whole Cake Island Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D41&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zou_Arc">Zou Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D42&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/58/Kid_Defeated.png/revision/latest?cb=20230626225108" class="image"><img alt="Kid Defeated" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="211" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kid Defeated.png" data-image-key="Kid_Defeated.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/58/Kid_Defeated.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230626225108" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/58/Kid_Defeated.png/revision/latest?cb=20230626225108" class="image"><img alt="Kid Defeated" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/58/Kid_Defeated.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230626225108" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="211" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kid Defeated.png" data-image-key="Kid_Defeated.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/58/Kid_Defeated.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230626225108" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kid_Defeated.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kid defeated and imprisoned.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the confrontation with Kaidou, Kid was severely beaten and imprisoned by the Emperor and his crew somewhere at <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a> as Kaidou commented on Luffy's actions at Dressrosa. At some point, Kid was relocated to the <a href="/wiki/Prisoner_Mine" title="Prisoner Mine">Prisoner Mine</a> in order to have his spirit broken.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Wano_Country_Saga">Wano Country Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D43&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><small>
</small></p><small><hr /></small><small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>The following events are <a href="/wiki/Canon#Non-Canon" title="Canon">Non-Canon</a> and therefore not considered part of the <a href="/wiki/Canon" title="Canon">Canon</a> story.</b></i></span>
</p></small><small><hr /></small>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="One_Piece:_Stampede">One Piece: Stampede</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D44&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d2/The_Worst_Generation_Together_Against_Bullet.png/revision/latest?cb=20210704115520" class="image"><img alt="The Worst Generation Together Against Bullet" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="The Worst Generation Together Against Bullet.png" data-image-key="The_Worst_Generation_Together_Against_Bullet.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d2/The_Worst_Generation_Together_Against_Bullet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210704115520" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d2/The_Worst_Generation_Together_Against_Bullet.png/revision/latest?cb=20210704115520" class="image"><img alt="The Worst Generation Together Against Bullet" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d2/The_Worst_Generation_Together_Against_Bullet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210704115520" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="The Worst Generation Together Against Bullet.png" data-image-key="The_Worst_Generation_Together_Against_Bullet.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d2/The_Worst_Generation_Together_Against_Bullet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210704115520" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:The_Worst_Generation_Together_Against_Bullet.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Worst Generation fight together against Douglas Bullet.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kid and his crew attended the <a href="/wiki/Pirates_Festival" title="Pirates Festival">Pirates Festival</a> on <a href="/wiki/Delta_Island" title="Delta Island">Delta Island</a>. He participated in the main event, the Treasure Race, safely sailing up the <a href="/wiki/Knock_Up_Stream" title="Knock Up Stream">Knock Up Stream</a> and landing on the central Treasure Island, where all the pirates raced for <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a>'s treasure, all the while battling other Worst Generation members. When <a href="/wiki/Buggy" title="Buggy">Buggy</a> ended up exposing himself after snatching the treasure, Kid and his crew chased after the Warlord. However, the Treasure Race was cut short, when someone threw a galleon at the island, destroying it, and sending everything plummeting back to the surface. When Kid realized that the one who did this was <a href="/wiki/Douglas_Bullet" title="Douglas Bullet">Douglas Bullet</a>, he was quite surprised. In the end, he gave into Bullet's taunting, and together with the other Worst Generation members (except for Zoro and Law) attacked the Demon Heir. At first the Worst Generation pirates managed to deal a few good blows on the veteran, but when the opponent revealed his <a href="/wiki/Gasha_Gasha_no_Mi" title="Gasha Gasha no Mi">Gasha Gasha no Mi</a> powers, the battle quickly ended in their defeat.
</p><p>Later, after Bullet was defeated, his crew along with the other Worst Generation pirates and several other crews attempted to breakthrough the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a> encirclement surrounding the island. They were able to successfully escape thanks to <a href="/wiki/Sabo" title="Sabo">Sabo</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ann" title="Ann">Ann</a> creating a blazing barrier to protect them.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup>
<small>
</small></p><small><hr /></small><small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>Concludes non-canon section.</b></i></span>
</p></small><small><hr /></small>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Wano_Country_Arc">Wano Country Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D45&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9a/Luffy_and_Kid_Imprisoned.png/revision/latest?cb=20230302154654" class="image"><img alt="Luffy and Kid Imprisoned" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Luffy and Kid Imprisoned.png" data-image-key="Luffy_and_Kid_Imprisoned.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9a/Luffy_and_Kid_Imprisoned.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230302154654" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9a/Luffy_and_Kid_Imprisoned.png/revision/latest?cb=20230302154654" class="image"><img alt="Luffy and Kid Imprisoned" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9a/Luffy_and_Kid_Imprisoned.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230302154654" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Luffy and Kid Imprisoned.png" data-image-key="Luffy_and_Kid_Imprisoned.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9a/Luffy_and_Kid_Imprisoned.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230302154654" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Luffy_and_Kid_Imprisoned.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kid and Luffy imprisoned at Udon.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the <a href="/wiki/Udon" title="Udon">Udon</a> region of <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano Country</a>, Kid was sitting in a cell of the Prisoner Mine when Luffy was thrown next to him. Both Kid and Luffy swore payback against Kaidou before they noticed each other.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup> A few days later, both of them were competing over who could do more work at the mine. <a href="/wiki/Dobon" title="Dobon">Dobon</a> then confronted the two over the amount of kibi dango rations they acquired. He prepared to discipline them by putting them both into his <a href="/wiki/SMILE" title="SMILE">hippo's mouth</a>. However, Kid and Luffy quickly knocked out Dobon and his hippo.<sup id="cite_ref-c926_34-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c926-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later, Kid overheard <a href="/wiki/Caribou" title="Caribou">Caribou</a> telling Luffy a rumor about how Kid's arm got cut off, and he interjected to correct the story. Kid and Luffy then argued over which one of them would take down Kaidou.<sup id="cite_ref-c928_9-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c928-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> At a later point, Kid somehow escaped from the prisoner mine.<sup id="cite_ref-c934_58-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c934-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2c/Kid_and_Kamazo_Undergo_Water_Torture.png/revision/latest?cb=20210816051616" class="image"><img alt="Kid and Kamazo Undergo Water Torture" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="210" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kid and Kamazo Undergo Water Torture.png" data-image-key="Kid_and_Kamazo_Undergo_Water_Torture.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2c/Kid_and_Kamazo_Undergo_Water_Torture.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210816051616" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2c/Kid_and_Kamazo_Undergo_Water_Torture.png/revision/latest?cb=20210816051616" class="image"><img alt="Kid and Kamazo Undergo Water Torture" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2c/Kid_and_Kamazo_Undergo_Water_Torture.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210816051616" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="210" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kid and Kamazo Undergo Water Torture.png" data-image-key="Kid_and_Kamazo_Undergo_Water_Torture.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2c/Kid_and_Kamazo_Undergo_Water_Torture.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210816051616" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kid_and_Kamazo_Undergo_Water_Torture.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kid and Kamazo undergo water torture.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kid later spotted Killer being escorted to the Prisoner Mines. He attempted to attack the escort only to be subdued and recaptured. After returning to the prison, Kid questioned Killer on what Kaidou had done to him and the fate of their crew, but Killer could not answer through his laughter and tears. <a href="/wiki/Queen" title="Queen">Queen</a> then subjugated them both to water torture and threatened to keep them submerged until Luffy and <a href="/wiki/Hyougoro" title="Hyougoro">Hyougoro</a> die in the Sumo Inferno.<sup id="cite_ref-c944_33-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c944-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> When <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a> was swinging Queen around, Kid and Killer were saved from drowning when Queen crashed into the contraption holding them and knocked them out of the water.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As Luffy and his allies from the <a href="/wiki/Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai_Alliance" title="Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance">Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance</a> were fighting against the Beasts Pirates, <a href="/wiki/Raizo" title="Raizo">Raizo</a> tossed some keys to Kid and Killer so they could release themselves. Kid sat there and watched as the chaos unfolded.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup> After the prison takeover had completed, Luffy offered Kid an alliance to defeat Kaidou. Kid rejected Luffy's offer, feeling betrayed by Apoo and Hawkins. He then took Killer with him and left the Prisoner Mines to find his other crewmates.<sup id="cite_ref-c950_20-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c950-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
