</p><p>On the day of the <a href="/wiki/Fire_Festival" title="Fire Festival">Fire Festival</a>, the Kid Pirates joined the Straw Hats and Heart Pirates in battling the Beasts Pirates' ships at Tokage Port. According to Kid, he met many ships and samurais on the other port that he found it difficult to set sail.<sup id="cite_ref-c974_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c974-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> After rescuing <a href="/wiki/Kin%27emon" title="Kin&#39;emon">Kin'emon</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Nine_Red_Scabbards" title="Nine Red Scabbards">group</a>, Kid and his crew were shocked to hear that Kaidou had formed an alliance with the <a href="/wiki/Big_Mom_Pirates" title="Big Mom Pirates">Big Mom Pirates</a>. Undeterred, Kid, Law, and Luffy destroyed a Beasts Pirates' ship together.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup> While dealing with the last enemy ship, he was surprised to see <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a>'s arrival and learned about the fish-man's joining with the Straw Hats.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/36/Punk_Gibson.png/revision/latest?cb=20230626222914" class="image"><img alt="Punk Gibson" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="182" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Punk Gibson.png" data-image-key="Punk_Gibson.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/36/Punk_Gibson.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230626222914" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/36/Punk_Gibson.png/revision/latest?cb=20230626222914" class="image"><img alt="Punk Gibson" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/36/Punk_Gibson.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230626222914" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="182" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Punk Gibson.png" data-image-key="Punk_Gibson.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/36/Punk_Gibson.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230626222914" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Punk_Gibson.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kid attacks Apoo.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When the Straw Hats took over the port in front of <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a>, Kid once again promised to be the one who would defeat Kaidou.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup> After disembarking on Onigashima, the Kid Pirates received Beasts Pirates disguises from Kin'emon.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup> As the alliance began their raid, the Kid Pirates went ahead of the Straw Hats, with Luffy and Zoro following after them.<sup id="cite_ref-c979_23-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c979-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>While sneaking through <a href="/wiki/Skull_Dome" title="Skull Dome">Skull Dome</a>'s Live Floor, Kid was surprised when Luffy and Zoro began causing a commotion. At first, he tried to ignore them in order to not bring unwanted attention to himself and his crew, but when he spotted Apoo, Kid decided to start fighting as well. As Apoo was distracted with attacking the two Straw Hats, Kid attacked Apoo for revenge.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> Apoo quickly recovered and retaliated, forcing Kid back. The situation became more chaotic as <a href="/wiki/Hatcha" title="Hatcha">Hatcha</a>, one of the <a href="/wiki/Numbers" title="Numbers">Numbers</a>, entered the fray. As Kid, Killer, Luffy, and Zoro ran to the castle, they were able to defend against Apoo's next attack by covering their ears.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Inside the castle, Kid and Killer got separated from their allies and found themselves fighting against several Gifters.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> As the Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance began their all-out war on the Beasts Pirates, Kid and Killer were aided by some of the rebels.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup> In preparation for the fight with Kaidou, Kid began using his magnetic powers to collect all the loose metallic objects on his way to the roof. As Kid and Killer reached the third level of the castle, the pile of metal had grown to fill the whole corridor.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7b/Supernovas_Confront_Kaidou_and_Big_Mom.png/revision/latest?cb=20230216005048" class="image"><img alt="Supernovas Confront Kaidou and Big Mom" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Supernovas Confront Kaidou and Big Mom.png" data-image-key="Supernovas_Confront_Kaidou_and_Big_Mom.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7b/Supernovas_Confront_Kaidou_and_Big_Mom.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230216005048" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7b/Supernovas_Confront_Kaidou_and_Big_Mom.png/revision/latest?cb=20230216005048" class="image"><img alt="Supernovas Confront Kaidou and Big Mom" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7b/Supernovas_Confront_Kaidou_and_Big_Mom.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230216005048" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Supernovas Confront Kaidou and Big Mom.png" data-image-key="Supernovas_Confront_Kaidou_and_Big_Mom.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7b/Supernovas_Confront_Kaidou_and_Big_Mom.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230216005048" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Supernovas_Confront_Kaidou_and_Big_Mom.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kid and the other Supernovas confront Kaidou and Big Mom.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The two later reached the roof, where they were soon joined by Law, Zoro, and Luffy as they prepared to fight against Kaidou and Big Mom.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup> Kid was briefly surprised when he saw Luffy hurt Kaidou. After Law sent the Red Scabbards and <a href="/wiki/Izou" title="Izou">Izou</a> to safety, Kid scoffed at the Surgeon of Death for being subservient to Luffy (since Law only acted after Luffy had asked) though Law insisted that he planned to help them either way. When Luffy challenged Kid and Law to a game of chicken in the face of Big Mom's attack, the two initially refused. However, following a small taunt from the Straw Hat captain, the two took up his challenge, with all of them ending up taking the full brunt of the attack. They quickly recovered, and the five members of the Worst Generation took a strike at Kaidou. However, Kaidou transformed into his <a href="/wiki/Uo_Uo_no_Mi,_Model:_Seiryu" title="Uo Uo no Mi, Model: Seiryu">dragon form</a> and joined Big Mom in the sky, preparing to battle.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Kaidou used a roar to unleash wind blades at his opponents. Kid's metal golem armor was struck but Kid remained unharmed. With his metal armor, Kid grabbed Kaidou and slammed him into the roof. Later, Big Mom unleashed a lightning storm at the five Supernovas. Kid managed to block some of her thunderbolts but was caught off guard by a lightning <a href="/wiki/Homies" title="Homies">homie</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup> After Luffy had pummeled Kaidou with Gomu Gomu no Kong Gatling, Kid and Killer tried to continue on the offensive, but Kaidou stopped them by creating some twisters. Zoro managed to slice through Kaidou's scales, but Kaidou responded by launching wind blades at the five Supernovas.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/ce/Kid_and_Law_Launch_Big_Mom_Away.png/revision/latest?cb=20210517185148" class="image"><img alt="Kid and Law Launch Big Mom Away" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="179" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kid and Law Launch Big Mom Away.png" data-image-key="Kid_and_Law_Launch_Big_Mom_Away.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/ce/Kid_and_Law_Launch_Big_Mom_Away.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210517185148" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/ce/Kid_and_Law_Launch_Big_Mom_Away.png/revision/latest?cb=20210517185148" class="image"><img alt="Kid and Law Launch Big Mom Away" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/ce/Kid_and_Law_Launch_Big_Mom_Away.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210517185148" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="179" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kid and Law Launch Big Mom Away.png" data-image-key="Kid_and_Law_Launch_Big_Mom_Away.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/ce/Kid_and_Law_Launch_Big_Mom_Away.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210517185148" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kid_and_Law_Launch_Big_Mom_Away.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kid and Law work together to remove Big Mom from the battlefield.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kid and the other Supernovas eventually agreed that they had to split up Big Mom and Kaidou somehow, otherwise they had no chance of winning.<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup> After surviving a combined attack from both Emperors thanks to Zoro's effort, Kid and Law elaborated a plan to separate Big Mom's special homies from her person. Kid used his powers to form a metal box so Law could teleport <a href="/wiki/Zeus" title="Zeus">Zeus</a> inside, while Zoro and Killer dealt with <a href="/wiki/Prometheus" title="Prometheus">Prometheus</a> and <a href="/wiki/Napoleon" title="Napoleon">Napoleon</a> respectively. Once Big Mom was fully disarmed, Kid shot metal spears at Big Mom, but was punched down into the ground by the Emperor in return. He, however, took the opportunity to grip Big Mom's arm with his own prosthetic arm, allowing him to Repel her up in the sky, from where Law managed to hit her with a boulder, throwing her off Onigashima.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Once Prometheus and Napoleon left Onigashima to rescue Big Mom, Kid and Killer followed them to the edge of the island. There, Kid noticed something strange happening to the clouds in the sky.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup> It turned out to be Big Mom creating a new homie, <a href="/wiki/Hera" title="Hera">Hera</a>, whose power she tested out on Kid and Killer as she headed back to Onigashima on Prometheus. Kid and Killer tried to avoid the way of Big Mom's <i>Fulgora</i> attack but were hit and sent flying back inside the <a href="/wiki/Skull_Dome" title="Skull Dome">Skull Dome</a>, on the third floor of Kaidou's Castle. Kid and Killer survived with few injuries and noticed that Big Mom was searching for them somewhere in the floor below. Kid ran off after her, but was stopped by Hawkins, his former ally and whom Kid considered a traitor. Killer told Kid to keep going while he stayed behind to keep Hawkins busy, which Kid complied.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/97/Kid_Slams_Big_Mom.png/revision/latest?cb=20210517181527" class="image"><img alt="Kid Slams Big Mom" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="211" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kid Slams Big Mom.png" data-image-key="Kid_Slams_Big_Mom.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/97/Kid_Slams_Big_Mom.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210517181527" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/97/Kid_Slams_Big_Mom.png/revision/latest?cb=20210517181527" class="image"><img alt="Kid Slams Big Mom" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/97/Kid_Slams_Big_Mom.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210517181527" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="211" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kid Slams Big Mom.png" data-image-key="Kid_Slams_Big_Mom.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/97/Kid_Slams_Big_Mom.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210517181527" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kid_Slams_Big_Mom.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kid slams Big Mom to the ground.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Once Kid reached the second floor, he noticed some of Kaidou's grunts alerting each other about Big Mom's location and headed towards the ruckus.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup> Kid eventually found Big Mom as she was about to strike down <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a>, <a href="/wiki/Usopp" title="Usopp">Usopp</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tama" class="mw-redirect" title="Tama">Tama</a>, using his <i>Punk Gibson</i> technique to block Big Mom's sword and then slam her down to the floor. Kid told the Straw Hats to leave Big Mom to him, as the latter recovered herself from the attack.<sup id="cite_ref-c1013_57-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1013-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> As Kid fought Big Mom, <a href="/wiki/Bao_Huang" title="Bao Huang">Bao Huang</a> announced that Luffy had died against Kaidou. Kid professed indifference to Luffy's fate,<sup id="cite_ref-c1014_39-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1014-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> but smiled when <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Momonosuke" title="Kouzuki Momonosuke">Momonosuke</a> confirmed the opposite in an announcement of his own.
</p><p>Shortly afterwards, Law made his way to the site of Kid's fight with Big Mom and proposed a temporary alliance with Kid to hold the Emperor back together.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup> During the fight, Kid struggled to stay on his feet due to mysterious injuries that kept springing up on his body. Unknown to Kid, these injuries were from Killer's attacks on Hawkins, who had <a href="/wiki/Wara_Wara_no_Mi" title="Wara Wara no Mi">linked</a> himself with Kid.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup> They were then surprised by the sudden interruption of Luffy riding a huge <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Momonosuke" title="Kouzuki Momonosuke">pink dragon</a> on his way back to the rooftop.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup> Later, Kid reacted to Luffy's broadcasted declaration to defeat Kaidou.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup> As the fight continued, Kid's pain reappeared, so Big Mom used Hera on Napoleon and was about to attack him, but Law defended Kid. However, the flames of Prometheus hit Law, who fell to the ground. Big Mom attacked the two pirates, injuring them further. Kid was perplexed by what was happening to him and disappointed that he might die pointlessly after finally reaching an Emperor. Once Killer severed Hawkins' link with Kid and defeated the Shinuchi, Kid quickly recovered and continued fighting Big Mom.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bc/Kid_Uses_Awakening_Against_Big_Mom.png/revision/latest?cb=20230402115532" class="image"><img alt="Kid Uses Awakening Against Big Mom" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kid Uses Awakening Against Big Mom.png" data-image-key="Kid_Uses_Awakening_Against_Big_Mom.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bc/Kid_Uses_Awakening_Against_Big_Mom.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230402115532" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bc/Kid_Uses_Awakening_Against_Big_Mom.png/revision/latest?cb=20230402115532" class="image"><img alt="Kid Uses Awakening Against Big Mom" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bc/Kid_Uses_Awakening_Against_Big_Mom.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230402115532" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kid Uses Awakening Against Big Mom.png" data-image-key="Kid_Uses_Awakening_Against_Big_Mom.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bc/Kid_Uses_Awakening_Against_Big_Mom.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230402115532" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kid_Uses_Awakening_Against_Big_Mom.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kid using his awakening on Big Mom.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Not finding any progress in causing major damage to Big Mom, Kid convinced Law to try utilizing their <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit#Awakening" title="Devil Fruit">awakenings</a> in order to change the tide of the fight. Kid was caught by a lightning blast from Big Mom that sent him back to the Live Floor in a freefall, with the Emperor following after Kid in order to finish him off in midair. Law, however, took the opportunity to activate his awakening and strike Big Mom from behind with <i>Shock Wille</i>, significantly injuring and distracting her long enough for Kid to initiate his own awakening and use <i>Punk Clash</i> to bury the Emperor underneath a multitude of steel beams ripped out from the framework of Kaidou's Castle.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup> This was, however, not sufficient to finish Big Mom off. Now truly angered, the Emperor stole the souls of several of Kaidou's minions in the Live Floor to power up her own special Homies and create new ones from the steel beams that previously crushed her. Having acknowledged Kid and Law's power, Big Mom sacrificed one year from her own lifespan in order to grow in size and power, all while daring the Worst Generation pirates to try and take her down. Not intimidated by Big Mom's new form, Kid declared that he would take the Emperor down no matter the cost.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Soon thereafter, Big Mom once again regained the upper hand, beating them up while mocking them about their crew's pleas to spare their lives. After Big Mom had punished their crews for pleading to her, she started to make her move towards the roof, viewing their fight as over. This would, however, give Law an advantage, as he was not defeated yet and exploited her ascension towards the roof, coating Kikoku with <i>K-Room</i> and stabbing her from right arm up to her face. He then unleashed <i>Shock Wille</i> onto her again, noticing she could not have been unharmed by this attack before. Right before he was about to be attacked by her newly created steel homies, they were attached towards Kid, who also rose up. After assimilating both the homies and surrounding metal, he confidently told Big Mom that nothing was impervious to damage before charging at Big Mom with <i>Punk Corna Dio</i>, ramming her into a wall. Both then once again assured Big Mom that they would not let her reach the roof, even if they died in the battle.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d8/Law_Defeats_Misery.png/revision/latest?cb=20230702032055" class="image"><img alt="Law Defeats Misery" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="251" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Law Defeats Misery.png" data-image-key="Law_Defeats_Misery.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d8/Law_Defeats_Misery.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702032055" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d8/Law_Defeats_Misery.png/revision/latest?cb=20230702032055" class="image"><img alt="Law Defeats Misery" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d8/Law_Defeats_Misery.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702032055" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="251" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Law Defeats Misery.png" data-image-key="Law_Defeats_Misery.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d8/Law_Defeats_Misery.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702032055" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Law_Defeats_Misery.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kid and Law finish off Big Mom.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kid then started arguing with Law as Big Mom recovered from their attacks. Law told Kid to prepare himself as the former would spend his last remaining stamina in a final attack. Kid took the opportunity to attack Big Mom once more, sticking her to one of the Live Floor's towers through his awakening. Big Mom, however, countered his maneuver and summoned a new homie, <a href="/wiki/Misery" title="Misery">Misery</a>, to burn Kid down. Kid was able to able to survive the attack and observed as Law pulled his final move. Taking advantage of the hole Law had produced with his awakening, Kid created an enormous railgun and fired a powerful projectile directly on Big Mom's stomach.
</p><p>However, this was not enough to finish off Big Mom, who activated her <i>Soul Pocus</i> in order to steal the souls of Kid and Law's crewmates. The technique, however, ended up being ineffective on both captains, who held no fear towards the Emperor. They then proceeded to silence and launch Big Mom out of Onigashima and directly into the crater Law had formed beforehand. With Big Mom falling victim to an explosion down below due to an explosive she accidentally detonated, a massively spent Kid and Law were heavily celebrated by their crews for the win.
</p><p>With only Luffy's fight left to finish, Kid waited for the battle to conclude, considering the possibility of Kaidou emerging as the winner. Once Kaidou descended from the rooftop and announced his victory over the Straw Hat captain, Kid lamented the outcome, but also declared that he would not go down without a fight as he prepared himself for combat once more. He was targeted by Kaidou's forces, but his crew protected him.
</p><p>Kid then noticed that Luffy was still alive through his Observation Haki and, after that, witnessed a <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_5_Techniques" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 5 Techniques">gigantic arm</a> descending from the ceiling and pulling Kaidou back to the rooftop, much to his shock, and more surprised that he witnessed Luffy's giant head after Kaidou hammered him from the roof. He also saw the samurai resigning themselves to a possible death but kept waiting for the final outcome of the fight<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup> and rejoiced alongside Killer when Kaidou's defeat was finally confirmed.<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>One week later, Kid and his crew oversaw the repairs of the <a href="/wiki/Victoria_Punk" title="Victoria Punk">Victoria Punk</a>, <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a> and <a href="/wiki/Polar_Tang" title="Polar Tang">Polar Tang</a> alongside <a href="/wiki/Usopp" title="Usopp">Usopp</a>, <a href="/wiki/Franky" title="Franky">Franky</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Heart_Pirates" title="Heart Pirates">Heart Pirates</a> at Tokage Port, with Kid trying to discourage his subordinates from getting too friendly with the Straw Hats. Apoo then arrived with a <a href="/wiki/Newspaper" title="Newspaper">newspaper</a> showing Kid's new <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>3,000,000,000 bounty as well as the <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">new</a> <a href="/wiki/Buggy" title="Buggy">members</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Four Emperors</a>. Angry about the contents of the paper, Kid rushed to the <a href="/wiki/Flower_Capital" title="Flower Capital">Flower Capital</a> to confront Luffy about the news but ended up forced into taking part in the festival's fireworks showcase against his will. Brushing off Luffy's attempts to socialize with him, Kid then showed the Straw Hat Captain the article about the new status the latter had been branded with.<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c9/Luffy_Law_and_Kid_at_Tokage_Port.png/revision/latest?cb=20240428232342" class="image"><img alt="Luffy Law and Kid at Tokage Port" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="150" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Luffy Law and Kid at Tokage Port.png" data-image-key="Luffy_Law_and_Kid_at_Tokage_Port.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c9/Luffy_Law_and_Kid_at_Tokage_Port.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240428232342" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c9/Luffy_Law_and_Kid_at_Tokage_Port.png/revision/latest?cb=20240428232342" class="image"><img alt="Luffy Law and Kid at Tokage Port" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c9/Luffy_Law_and_Kid_at_Tokage_Port.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240428232342" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="150" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Luffy Law and Kid at Tokage Port.png" data-image-key="Luffy_Law_and_Kid_at_Tokage_Port.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c9/Luffy_Law_and_Kid_at_Tokage_Port.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240428232342" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Luffy_Law_and_Kid_at_Tokage_Port.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kid, Luffy and Law deciding on what routes to take.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>A few days later, while their crews were loading up cargo at Tokage Port, Kid, Luffy and Law tried to decide between themselves new <a href="/wiki/Log_Pose" title="Log Pose">routes</a> for each of them to follow, with Kid eventually setting for the easternmost path after beating Luffy at straws. Annoyed with Luffy's childishness, Kid took the opportunity to show and then explain to him a leaflet illustrating the <a href="/wiki/Cross_Guild" title="Cross Guild">Cross Guild</a>, a new group formed by <a href="/wiki/Buggy" title="Buggy">Buggy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Crocodile" title="Crocodile">Crocodile</a> and <a href="/wiki/Dracule_Mihawk" title="Dracule Mihawk">Dracule Mihawk</a>, much to the Straw Hat captain's shock. Kid also ended up receiving a rubbing of Wano's Road Poneglyph from Law for his decisive role in the raid. Kid and Killer then started discussing the serious possibility of looking around for a <a href="/wiki/Hinokizu" title="Hinokizu">mysterious man with a "burn mark"</a> that they felt could be key in the fight for the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece" title="One Piece">One Piece</a>, something that piqued Luffy's curiosity, much to Kid's amusement.<sup id="cite_ref-c1056_47-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1056-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>With his crew ready to set sail, the Kid Pirates departed from Wano, but not before Kid himself mocked Luffy and Law one last time and goaded them into leaving the country by jumping off the Climbing Koi Waterfall.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Final_Saga">Final Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D46&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Egghead_Arc">Egghead Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D47&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a8/Shanks_Defeats_Kid.png/revision/latest?cb=20240714021139" class="image"><img alt="Shanks Defeats Kid" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="213" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Shanks Defeats Kid.png" data-image-key="Shanks_Defeats_Kid.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a8/Shanks_Defeats_Kid.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240714021139" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a8/Shanks_Defeats_Kid.png/revision/latest?cb=20240714021139" class="image"><img alt="Shanks Defeats Kid" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a8/Shanks_Defeats_Kid.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240714021139" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="213" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Shanks Defeats Kid.png" data-image-key="Shanks_Defeats_Kid.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a8/Shanks_Defeats_Kid.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240714021139" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Shanks_Defeats_Kid.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kid is defeated by Shanks in one blow.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Following the sea route their captain chose back at Wano, the Kid Pirates eventually reached their next destination, <a href="/wiki/Elbaph" title="Elbaph">Elbaph</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup> Shortly after their arrival, they encountered the <a href="/wiki/Red_Hair_Pirates" title="Red Hair Pirates">Red Hair Pirates</a> and the latter's allied crews, thus prompting Kid and his crew to prepare for battle.<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup> When the battle began, Kid immediately formed his Damned Punk. Using his Future Sight, Shanks beheld a catastrophic scene unfold as Kid's attack destroyed and slaughtered hundreds in one go. Refusing to let this happen and harboring strong disgust towards Kid for going so overboard on collateral damage, Kid was immediately struck down in a single blow with Shanks' <a href="/wiki/Gryphon#Techniques" title="Gryphon">Kamusari</a>. In the anime, it was shown that the damage was both from Shanks' Kamusari and the Damned Punk releasing its stored energy after Shanks sliced Kid's weapon. His crew then pleaded for mercy and handed over their Poneglyph rubbings. However, as Shanks left the Victoria Punk, it was then split in half by Dorry and Brogy's Hakoku, and the crew sank with the ship.<sup id="cite_ref-c1079_13-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1079-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup><br style="clear:both;" />
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Anime_and_Manga_Differences">Anime and Manga Differences</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D50&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>When Kid, Law, and their respective crews encountered a Pacifista, it is currently not specified whether this one was Kuma or not in the manga and are left with a cliffhanger. In the anime, this one was a regular Pacifista and the pirates were given some scenes fighting it. When it seemed that they defeated the Pacifista, it got back up and resumed its attack, essentially leaving the same cliffhanger as in the manga.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Translation_and_Dub_Issues">Translation and Dub Issues</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D51&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/82/Kid%27s_Name_Romanization.png/revision/latest?cb=20110106123821" class="image"><img alt="Kid&#39;s Name Romanization" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="99" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kid&#39;s Name Romanization.png" data-image-key="Kid%27s_Name_Romanization.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/82/Kid%27s_Name_Romanization.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20110106123821" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/82/Kid%27s_Name_Romanization.png/revision/latest?cb=20110106123821" class="image"><img alt="Kid&#39;s Name Romanization" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/82/Kid%27s_Name_Romanization.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20110106123821" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="99" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kid&#39;s Name Romanization.png" data-image-key="Kid%27s_Name_Romanization.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/82/Kid%27s_Name_Romanization.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20110106123821" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kid%27s_Name_Romanization.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kid's name as romanized in his introduction.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Even though the correct romanization for his name was shown in his introduction, the "d" in "Kid" was cut off, leading many people to believe that there was more of his name, and used "Kidd" for his name, basing it on the pirate William Kidd, the confirmed basis for the name. Eventually, in <a href="/wiki/Chapter_594" title="Chapter 594">Chapter 594</a>, it was confirmed to be "Kid".<sup id="cite_ref-c594p11_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c594p11-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_Concepts">Early Concepts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D52&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 250px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/77/Early_Kid.png/revision/latest?cb=20230921134016" class="image"><img alt="Early Kid" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="250" height="177" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Early Kid.png" data-image-key="Early_Kid.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/77/Early_Kid.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230921134016" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/77/Early_Kid.png/revision/latest?cb=20230921134016" class="image"><img alt="Early Kid" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/77/Early_Kid.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230921134016" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="250" height="177" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Early Kid.png" data-image-key="Early_Kid.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/77/Early_Kid.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230921134016" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Early_Kid.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Early designs for Kid from One Piece Magazine Vol.8.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Magazine_Vol.8" title="One Piece Magazine Vol.8">eighth</a> volume of <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Magazine" title="One Piece Magazine">One Piece Magazine</a>, several early design sketches for Kid were revealed, some of which included different variations of his hairstyle.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup><br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Merchandise">Merchandise</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D53&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_Appearances">Other Appearances</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D58&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_Media">Other Media</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D59&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 150px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/ce/Kid_Premier_Show.png/revision/latest?cb=20201219015201" class="image"><img alt="Kid Premier Show" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="150" height="121" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kid Premier Show.png" data-image-key="Kid_Premier_Show.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/ce/Kid_Premier_Show.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20201219015201" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/ce/Kid_Premier_Show.png/revision/latest?cb=20201219015201" class="image"><img alt="Kid Premier Show" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/ce/Kid_Premier_Show.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20201219015201" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="150" height="121" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kid Premier Show.png" data-image-key="Kid_Premier_Show.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/ce/Kid_Premier_Show.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20201219015201" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kid_Premier_Show.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kid in Premier Show 2014.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>In <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Premier_Show#One_Piece_Premier_Show_2014" title="One Piece Premier Show">One Piece Premier Show 2014</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bildy" title="Bildy">Bildy</a> makes a <a href="/wiki/Kone_Kone_no_Mi" title="Kone Kone no Mi">fake version</a> of Kid to fight as a general of the <a href="/wiki/DX_Marines" title="DX Marines">DX Marines</a>.<br style="clear:both;" /></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D60&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Kid shares some things with the other members of the <a href="/wiki/Worst_Generation" title="Worst Generation">Worst Generation</a>:
<ul><li>He, <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</a> are the only known members who can use <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a>.
<ul><li>Also, he, <a href="/wiki/Sengoku" title="Sengoku">Sengoku</a> and <a href="/wiki/Boa_Hancock" title="Boa Hancock">Boa Hancock</a> are the only characters confirmed to have Supreme King Haki, but never shown any usage of it the manga yet.</li></ul></li>
<li>He, Monkey D. Luffy, and <a href="/wiki/Trafalgar_D._Water_Law" title="Trafalgar D. Water Law">Trafalgar D. Water Law</a> are the only known members to have <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit#Awakening" title="Devil Fruit">awakened</a> their Devil Fruits.</li></ul></li>
<li>When Kid speaks of his experiences in the Grand Line, he mentions killing everyone who dared to laugh at him and his dream to find the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece" title="One Piece">One Piece</a> and become the next <a href="/wiki/Pirate#Pirate_King" title="Pirate">Pirate King</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup> In contrast, when the <a href="/wiki/Bellamy_Pirates" title="Bellamy Pirates">Bellamy Pirates</a> started laughing at the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> for being "dreamers", instead of responding to <a href="/wiki/Bellamy" title="Bellamy">Bellamy</a>'s mockery, Luffy claimed that it was not a battle worth fighting, following the example taught to him by <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>In the 6th <a href="/wiki/Popularity_Polls" title="Popularity Polls">fan poll</a> of most popular characters, Kid was ranked 37th, which makes him the second most popular non-Straw Hat Supernova, behind Trafalgar D. Water Law. He managed to retain this distinction despite falling 19 places after ranking 18th in the 5th fan poll. In the 4th and 7th fan polls, Kid ranked 15th and 23rd, respectively.</li>
<li>Kid being incarcerated in the region of <a href="/wiki/Udon" title="Udon">Udon</a> could be considered ironic since curry udon is his least favorite food. He shares this aspect with Killer, who also gets briefly imprisoned and tortured in the same location.</li>
<li>The water torture that Kid and Killer were subjected to in the <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country_Arc" title="Wano Country Arc">Wano Country Arc</a> is a version of the old Japanese torture and execution method known as <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ana-tsurushi" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:ana-tsurushi">ana-tsurushi</a></i>, or "reverse hanging".
<ul><li>Interestingly, the real-life William Kidd was executed through a very similar method: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/gibbeting" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:gibbeting">gibbeting</a> or being "hanged in chains".</li></ul></li>
<li>Kid shares his <a href="/wiki/Epithet" title="Epithet">epithet</a> of "Captain" with <a href="/wiki/John" title="John">John</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kuro" title="Kuro">Kuro</a>.</li>
<li>Kid enjoys summer on <a href="/wiki/Island_Climatic_Types" title="Island Climatic Types">Summer Islands</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="SBS-Based_Trivia">SBS-Based Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FEustass_Kid%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D61&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>Kid's birthday, January 10, comes from his name since 1-10 can be derived from Kid-do.<sup id="cite_ref-Birth_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Birth-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Kid's surname and name were taken from two real-life pirates. His surname Eustass was taken from 13th century French pirate and mercenary <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Eustace_the_Monk" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Eustace the Monk">Eustace the Monk</a>, and his name Kid from 17th century Scottish pirate and privateer, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Kidd" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Kidd">William Kidd</a>, who was also nicknamed "Captain".<sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>A fan asked Oda who would win if Kid, Monkey D. Luffy, and Trafalgar D. Water Law played a game of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rock_paper_scissors" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Rock paper scissors">Rock paper scissors</a>, if it would be Luffy because he can <a href="/wiki/Haki/Observation_Haki#Future_Vision" title="Haki/Observation Haki">see the future</a>, and Oda answered that while Luffy can indeed see the future and could do that to win, he hates cheating, so Oda does not think Luffy would look into the future. At the end, Oda added that they do not get along very well with each other, so they would end up fighting no matter who wins.<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Kid's favorite food is cabbage rolls. His least favorite food is curry udon because he and <a href="/wiki/Killer" title="Killer">Killer</a> were beaten up by Victoria Shiruton Doruyanaika for laughing at her when she spilled curry udon all over herself.<sup id="cite_ref-sbs87_35-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs87-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Kid's animal resemblance is a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_Fighting_Bull" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Spanish Fighting Bull">fighting bull</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-sbs95_122-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs95-122">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>If One Piece was set in the real world, then Kid would be from Scotland, just like Killer. This reflects his namesake, William Kidd.<sup id="cite_ref-sbs88_123-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs88-123">&#91;123&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>When a fan asked which flower Kid resembles the most, Oda answered he most resembles a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/tulip" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:tulip">tulip</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-sbs95_122-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs95-122">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>If Kid was not a pirate, then he would be a weapons merchant.<sup id="cite_ref-sbs88_123-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs88-123">&#91;123&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Kid's hobbies are listening to music and collecting weapons.<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
